
-----title
仙游 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5a6020fbb5b145f682994899b4c0af6c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5a6020fbb5b145f682994899b4c0af6c");'><span id='5a6020fbb5b145f682994899b4c0af6c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1216')">1184-1216年</a>，1-33岁</div><div id='5a6020fbb5b145f682994899b4c0af6c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　是年，王迈生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1193')">1185-1193年</a>　少居家乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1197')">1194-1197年</a>　居乡求学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年</a>　已读书，读书之堂曰“养正堂”，真德秀有《养正堂记》,<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1203')">1199-1203年</a>　居乡求学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1204&endYear=1204')">1204年</a>　贡于乡。以文谒傅诚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1205&endYear=1213')">1205-1213年</a>　开门授业。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1214&endYear=1214')">1214年9月9日</a>　九月九日，日食，有诗纪之。作品：《甲戌九月日有食之纪异三十韵》<div id='poem_56903' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56903' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56903?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甲戌九月日有食之纪异三十韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1214年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_56903")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56903_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56903'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56903'>甲戌九月秋，朔旦见灾眚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56903'>孛彗犯太阳，凄凄如月冷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56903'>方其始亏时，宛然虫食皿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56903'>食之至于既，当空悬黑饼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56903'>髣髴存轮圈，中陷犹枯井。<div id='poem_sentence_4_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_56903'>云间星昼见，草木森弄影。<div id='poem_sentence_5_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_56903'>天地寂无声，疑似非人境。<div id='poem_sentence_6_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_56903'>问之道旁翁，欲语喉先哽。<div id='poem_sentence_7_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_56903'>翁今九十馀，眼未见此景。<div id='poem_sentence_8_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_56903'>爰有虮虱臣，拜跪泪沾领。<div id='poem_sentence_9_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_56903'>天高听则卑，宜鉴愚臣请。<div id='poem_sentence_10_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_56903'>日者阳之宗，千古光常炳。<div id='poem_sentence_11_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_56903'>此日何不臧，臣心忧耿耿。<div id='poem_sentence_12_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_56903'>或者天爱君，先事示之警。<div id='poem_sentence_13_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_56903'>流金为汤戒，洚水为尧儆。<div id='poem_sentence_14_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_56903'>虽重一时忧，何伤天历永。<div id='poem_sentence_15_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_56903'>吾君今尧汤，四海元元幸。<div id='poem_sentence_16_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_56903'>公道大开明，朝列肃而整。<div id='poem_sentence_17_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_56903'>祇恐万一间，左右容憸悻。<div id='poem_sentence_18_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_56903'>方秋阴用事，阳微阴渐逞。<div id='poem_sentence_19_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_56903'>不去谗慝根，惧作忠良阱。<div id='poem_sentence_20_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_56903'>天乃出怪异，意欲悟观省。<div id='poem_sentence_21_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_56903'>吾国必有人，伏蒲输骨鲠。<div id='poem_sentence_22_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_56903'>吾君必开纳，小心知畏谨。<div id='poem_sentence_23_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_56903'>阳政必日修，阴邪必痛屏。<div id='poem_sentence_24_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_56903'>天其终仁爱，悔过在俄顷。<div id='poem_sentence_25_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_56903'>大叫天上人，齐唤金乌醒。<div id='poem_sentence_26_56903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_56903'></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_56903_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1215&endYear=1215')">1215年</a>　开门授业。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1216&endYear=1216')">1216年</a>　再贡。作品：《丙子再荐谢太守启》<div id='poem_1304390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304390?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙子再荐谢太守启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1216年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304390")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304390_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304390'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304390'>少而好赋，尝见齿于贤书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304390_comment'></div>壮当封侯，尚何颜于文屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304390_comment'></div>偶辱明有司之选，重书新进士之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304390_comment'></div>况弟子之贤于师，既叨首荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304390_comment'></div>而他人不如同父，又获联名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304390_comment'></div>人称之以为美谈，己当之独有惭色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304390_comment'></div>伏念某箕裘晚出，门户早衰，缀文几至于呕肝，苦学惟知于尝胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304390_comment'></div>十年以前之志，岂信富贵之在天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304390_comment'></div>累战不利之馀，方知穷达之有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304390_comment'></div>开门授业，仰屋著书，谓若无所用于一时，亦将垂不朽于千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304390_comment'></div>属槐花之近目，陡觉激昂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304390_comment'></div>认杨叶之旧穿，未知中否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304390_comment'></div>赋不工于吐凤，墨误点以成蝇，设非以后场而见收，几乎为文衡之所弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304390_comment'></div>荆山之璞获售，合浦之珠复还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304390_comment'></div>亲望因得以少宽，朋旧亦怜其才遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304390_comment'></div>靖言侥倖，亶有夤缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304390_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官宗主斯文之盟，作成多士之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304390_comment'></div>治平有第一誉，已彻公车；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304390_comment'></div>举送馀四十人，亲为劝驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304390_comment'></div>致令么么，再预甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304390_comment'></div>某敢不益加驽钝之鞭，勉赴功名之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304390_comment'></div>天其或者，道之行欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304390_comment'></div>雁序联飞，伫见齐名于雁塔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304390_comment'></div>龙门高远，未知谁占于龙头。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1304390_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1216&endYear=1216')">1216年</a>　是年有诗。作品：《丙子诏后需捷四绝》<div id='poem_70973' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_70973' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/70973?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙子诏后需捷四绝<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1216年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_70973")'>王迈</a></span><br id='poem_sentence_0_70973'>一面飞来打叠秋，农场已筑管无忧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_70973_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_70973'>吾侬种殖三年学，未省书田还有收。<div id='poem_sentence_1_70973_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_70973'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_70973_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_70971' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_70971' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/70971?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1216年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_70971_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_70971'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_70971'>促织墙阴唧唧吟，早催衣褐上寒砧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_70971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_70971'>砧声似助蛩声切，勾引征夫万里心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_70971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_70971'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_70971_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_70972' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_70972' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/70972?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1216年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_70972_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_70972'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_70972'>战罢归来月再盈，悬知得失系心旌。<div id='poem_sentence_0_70972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_70972'>应门稚子占蛛信，刺绣佳人听鹊声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_70972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_70972'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_70972_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_70974' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_70974' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/70974?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_0_70974'>胜负相持日已多，看棋人已烂仙柯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_70974_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_70974'>淮淝非久捷书到，还折门前屐齿么。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1217&endYear=1217')">1217年6月</a>　归乡，有诗别同年蒋有秋。作品：《丁丑同蒋力父东归至城诗以别之》<div id='poem_71227' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71227' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_71227'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71227'>发轫神皋愁热甚，解骖乡井得凉多。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71227'>半生相托左右手，一日同收甲乙科。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71227'>老我已锄年少习，期君共守岁寒柯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71227'>荣华富贵邯郸枕，惟孝惟忠久不磨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71227'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_71227_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1217&endYear=1217')">1217年12月</a>　腊月，有《跋陈君保作喆藏赵忠定公帖（一）》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1218&endYear=1218')">1218年</a>　待任在家。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2fc86f000c464e30979eb718dbaf3cc3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2fc86f000c464e30979eb718dbaf3cc3");'><span id='2fc86f000c464e30979eb718dbaf3cc3_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1222&endYear=1222')">1222年</a>　春，丁内艰。作品：《白发叹》<div id='poem_56905' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56905' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56905?labeling=true' target='_blank'>白发叹<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1222年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_56905")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56905_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56905'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56905'>日月转四时，团团辗清昊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56905'>人生一世间，轻尘栖弱草。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56905'>寒暑不相贷，容鬓岂常好。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56905'>嗟予涉世纷，闻道苦不早。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56905'>尘劳纵掀簸，冉冉风中葆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_56905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_56905'>行年将四十，素标已插脑。<div id='poem_sentence_5_56905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_56905'>星星才数茎，烂熳色胜缟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_56905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_56905'>耘镊虽暂无，安能遏衰槁。<div id='poem_sentence_7_56905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_56905'>黄精似可饵，已白恐难扫。<div id='poem_sentence_8_56905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_56905'>幸有琴心文，真诀堪却老。<div id='poem_sentence_9_56905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_56905'>华池溉隐芝，青青可常保。<div id='poem_sentence_10_56905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_56905'>斯理不吾欺，从今勤探讨。<div id='poem_sentence_11_56905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_56905'>要当验他时，难为常人道。<div id='poem_sentence_12_56905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_56905'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_56905_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56904' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56904' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56904?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1222年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56904_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56904'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56904'>青铜作明鉴，皎皎铺晴昊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56904'>照我沐初晞，几缕经霜草。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56904'>本无适俗韵，颇识林园好。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56904'>何为浪自苦，落得衰颜早。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56904'>悬知日夜改，青丝成素葆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_56904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_56904'>达人遗世累，土木视肝脑。<div id='poem_sentence_5_56904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_56904'>那于形骸间，计校玄与缟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_56904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_56904'>彼独何人哉，而我叹枯槁。<div id='poem_sentence_7_56904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_56904'>壮年不可挽，过日如霜扫。<div id='poem_sentence_8_56904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_56904'>但有岁寒心，不逐冰霜老。<div id='poem_sentence_9_56904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_56904'>誓开三径荒，种艺杂庸保。<div id='poem_sentence_10_56904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_56904'>虽无大药资，尚得恣幽讨。<div id='poem_sentence_11_56904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_56904'>此外尽悠悠，置之不复道。<div id='poem_sentence_12_56904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_56904'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_56904_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1223&endYear=1223')">1223年</a>　居家丁内艰。作品：《四十自寿》<div id='poem_56902' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56902' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56902?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四十自寿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1223年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_56902")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56902_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56902'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56902'>前四十年非，追之已莫返。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56902'>后四十年是，图之良未晚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56902'>水涸自见涘，木落知见本。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56902'>善者契吾机，今复犹不远。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56902'>养生先节欲，葆粹在惩忿。<div id='poem_sentence_4_56902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_56902'>圣贤人可为，勿使善恶混。<div id='poem_sentence_5_56902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_56902'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_56902_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1223&endYear=1223')">1223年12月30日</a>　除夕刘克庄自桂林被召到莆，作词呈之。作品：《贺新郎•呈刘后村，时自桂林被召到莆，又遭烦言》<div id='poem_71376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71376?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新郎<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>呈刘后村，时自桂林被召到莆，又遭烦言</a><span class='authorDate'>（1223年12月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_71376")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_71376_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_71376'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71376'>出了罗浮洞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71376'>有多情、梅花雪片，殷勤相送。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71376'>见说翛然琴鹤外，诗压牛腰较重。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71376'>又管甚、群儿嘲弄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71376'>岭海三年持翠节，料无时、不作家山梦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_71376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_71376'>驰玉勒，归金凤<span class='inlineComment2'>（金凤池，乃所居也。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_71376_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_71376'>一门朱紫环昆仲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_71376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_71376'>看阶庭、森森兰玉，慈颜欢动。<div id='poem_sentence_7_71376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_71376'>宰相时来须著做，且舞莱衣侍奉。<div id='poem_sentence_8_71376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_71376'>却不信、大才难用。<div id='poem_sentence_9_71376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_71376'>时事多艰人物少，便中兴、谁辨浯溪颂。<div id='poem_sentence_10_71376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_71376'>更大厦，要梁栋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_71376_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1224&endYear=1224')">1224年</a>　居家丁内艰。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e8a46e6c6f1f4a2f8da995892c558c20_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e8a46e6c6f1f4a2f8da995892c558c20");'><span id='e8a46e6c6f1f4a2f8da995892c558c20_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1229&endYear=1231')">1229-1231年</a>，46-48岁</div><div id='e8a46e6c6f1f4a2f8da995892c558c20' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1229&endYear=1229')">1229年10月</a>　归家，过建宁府、南剑州，亲亲睹兵乱，作诗纪之。作品：《亲旧问盗作诗四十韵以答之亦可备野史之录》<div id='poem_56930' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56930' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56930?labeling=true' target='_blank'>亲旧问盗作诗四十韵以答之亦可备野史之录</a><span class='authorDate'>（1229年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_56930")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56930_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56930'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56930'>我来自京师，己丑之十月。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56930'>道之建剑间，行行遇兵卒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56930'>问之何为行，对言声哽咽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56930'>初只因临汀，盐商时出没。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56930'>县官事张皇，星夜闻帅钺。<div id='poem_sentence_4_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_56930'>帅出乃捕兵，此曹辄猖獗。<div id='poem_sentence_5_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_56930'>加之江西寇，恃崄护巢穴。<div id='poem_sentence_6_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_56930'>向来误杀降，贻祸今尤烈。<div id='poem_sentence_7_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_56930'>合党肆纷披，交锋争桀黠。<div id='poem_sentence_8_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_56930'>聚落四百村，室庐遭毁爇。<div id='poem_sentence_9_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_56930'>转徙临昭阳，孤城危一发。<div id='poem_sentence_10_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_56930'>帅方实归装，视此苦不切。<div id='poem_sentence_11_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_56930'>惟漕暨庾台，协心图扑灭。<div id='poem_sentence_12_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_56930'>移文责十连，义激词语辣。<div id='poem_sentence_13_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_56930'>就檄刘权军，专城植铩𢧕。<div id='poem_sentence_14_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_56930'>又有一老尉，贾勇抗鸱鹘。<div id='poem_sentence_15_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_56930'>赖此所居民，犹苟旦暮活。<div id='poem_sentence_16_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_56930'>我闻此卒言，忧愤中肠热。<div id='poem_sentence_17_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_56930'>及归抵吾庐，保伍亦团结。<div id='poem_sentence_18_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_56930'>或恐汀邵寇，馀烬尚分裂。<div id='poem_sentence_19_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_56930'>或疑鼠狗徒，乘间敢窃发。<div id='poem_sentence_20_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_56930'>吾乡号乐国，目不见寸铁。<div id='poem_sentence_21_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_56930'>一闻钲鼓声，缩头畏如鳖。<div id='poem_sentence_22_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_56930'>新岁或讹言，城居竟搬挈。<div id='poem_sentence_23_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_56930'>丁男肩欲赪，稚女足不袜。<div id='poem_sentence_24_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_56930'>相顾莫为谋，去守将安决。<div id='poem_sentence_25_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_56930'>汝知诲盗谁，吾能为汝说。<div id='poem_sentence_26_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_56930'>年来民贼多，田里困根括。<div id='poem_sentence_27_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_56930'>单丁火亦追，逃户租尽刷。<div id='poem_sentence_28_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_56930'>猛虎政太苛，攘鸡手已滑。<div id='poem_sentence_29_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_56930'>剥床忍及肤，椎肌惨见血。<div id='poem_sentence_30_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_56930'>吏肥富薰天，民贫怨刻骨。<div id='poem_sentence_31_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_56930'>及此皆幸灾，狺险何聒聒。<div id='poem_sentence_32_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_56930'>古来盗贼兴<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，官吏去饕餮。<div id='poem_sentence_33_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_56930'>大者籍其家，小亦寘重罚。<div id='poem_sentence_34_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_56930'>人心知是非，端可以理折。<div id='poem_sentence_35_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_56930'>民贼尽芟夷，虽赏之不窃。<div id='poem_sentence_36_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_56930'></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_56930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_56930'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_33_56930_0'>⑴ 原按：此与下句不接，考次首和韵，此处脱六句。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_56930_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1230&endYear=1230')">1230年8月</a>　免官闲居。八月，有诗送赵孟坚。作品：《送莆守赵孟坚汝固司舶温陵》<div id='poem_71289' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71289' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71289?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送莆守赵孟坚汝固司舶温陵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1230年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_71289")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_71289_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_71289'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71289'>君不见有唐元结守舂陵，湘湖一道盗纵横。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71289'>独元所治一无犯，镇抚孤垒如金城。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71289'>又不见祁公曾作乾州牧，移镇凤翔何迅速。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71289'>两州之民境上争，先把州麾后钧轴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71289'>使君来莆全似元，精明旗帜张辕门。<div id='poem_sentence_4_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_71289'>威风惠雨相劘拂，鼠辈不敢闯吾藩。<div id='poem_sentence_5_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_71289'>使君去莆仍似杜，截镫遮留喧道路。<div id='poem_sentence_6_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_71289'>吾莆赤子方有依，泉何为者争吾父。<div id='poem_sentence_7_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_71289'>我将软语劳莆人，此地幸与泉为邻。<div id='poem_sentence_8_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_71289'>刁斗相闻邹近鲁，瘠肥不比越视秦。<div id='poem_sentence_9_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_71289'>使君风采压人望，莆亦倚泉为保障。<div id='poem_sentence_10_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_71289'>渠魁缚致藁街前，四野腥膻行涤荡。<div id='poem_sentence_11_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_71289'>长淮以北多风埃，社稷正倚经纶才。<div id='poem_sentence_12_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_71289'>出平西贼入衮绣，一韩一范何人哉。<div id='poem_sentence_13_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_71289'>书生自顾老无力，不能从公取俘馘。<div id='poem_sentence_14_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_71289'>愿将诗颂纪中兴，浓墨大字书浯石。<div id='poem_sentence_15_71289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_71289'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_71289_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1231&endYear=1231')">1231年</a>　免官闲居。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a84388c810fd4ba6aaff5070d806a564_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a84388c810fd4ba6aaff5070d806a564");'><span id='a84388c810fd4ba6aaff5070d806a564_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1240')">1238-1240年</a>，55-57岁</div><div id='a84388c810fd4ba6aaff5070d806a564' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　免官闲居故里。夏，有跋文。作品：《跋大庾令赵宗华时棣藏诸公帖》<div id='poem_71203' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71203' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71203?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋大庾令赵宗华时棣藏诸公帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_71203")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_71203_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_71203'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71203'>数帖凡经几世藏，字漫黑暗欠装潢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71203'>孰贤孰否人千载，遗臭遗芳纸半张。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71203'>愤世疾邪成怒骂，怀忠爱直转凄凉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71203'>吾曹留面要相见，莫使人能议短长<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71203'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_71203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_71203'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_71203_0'>⑴ 自注：王梅溪云：吾曹离合不常，要须他日留面相见。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_71203_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>　免官闲居。赵涯知泉州，有诗送之。作品：《送赵伯泳涯侍郎守温陵》<div id='poem_71125' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71125' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71125?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送赵伯泳涯侍郎守温陵<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_71125")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_71125_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_71125'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71125'>泉是梅溪遗爱乡，老倪复此种甘棠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71125'>后来荐报西山政，归去全无南物装。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71125'>籍甚三贤皆法从，勉哉一赵继循良。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71125'>万安桥上传佳话，七十年间四侍郎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71125'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_71125_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_71287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71287?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_71287_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_71287'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71287'>西山无物与泉民，底使民如父母亲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71287'>凡日用间无不敬，满腔子里尽吾仁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71287'>我熏知见香犹旧，公涤中和印一新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71287'>愿广桐乡依恋意，寒泉秋菊祀千春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71287'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_71287_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>　免官闲居。赵涯知泉州，又填词送之。作品：《贺新郎•送赵伯泳侍郎守温陵》<div id='poem_71374' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71374' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71374?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新郎<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>送赵伯泳侍郎守温陵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_71374")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_71374_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_71374'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71374'>忆昔同时召。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71374'>正青山、亲提玉尺，量材廊庙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71374'>当日班行比元祐，北玉西珠照耀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71374'>一转首、宫商移调。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71374'>君自乌台登骑省，觉精神、风采增清峭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_71374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_71374'>数贤者，一不肖。<div id='poem_sentence_5_71374_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_71374'>酒酣耳热惟长啸。<div id='poem_sentence_6_71374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_71374'>便翩翩、辍班荷橐，一麾闽峤。<div id='poem_sentence_7_71374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_71374'>堪笑狂生无用处，垂老云耕月钓。<div id='poem_sentence_8_71374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_71374'>这富贵、非由人要。<div id='poem_sentence_9_71374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_71374'>畴昔评君如玉雪，好翛然、琴鹤风尘表。<div id='poem_sentence_10_71374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_71374'>清献后，又有赵。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_71374_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>　免官闲居。夏，为方应龙撰墓志。作品：《莆阳方梅叔墓志铭》<div id='poem_1304614' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304614' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304614?labeling=true' target='_blank'>莆阳方梅叔墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉熙三年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304614")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304614_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304614'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304614'>莆品丁之家，方为著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304614_comment'></div>端人绅士，层见叠出，有位公卿立修名姱节于朝者，有任牧伯连帅扬仁风义槩于方外者，馀挟一能一艺，多奋拔于乡于学，于天子之庭，故莆人有「无方不成榜」之谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304614_comment'></div>独梅叔君怀瑾握瑜，足迹半湖海，而天无老眼，命压人头，偃蹇不得志，赍恨下泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304614_comment'></div>唐人所谓「直教桂子落坟上，生得一枝魂始消」者，非君之谓欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304614_comment'></div>君少受知于叔祖少卿公铨，仕衡阳日，君以弟子为宾客，自书札外未尝毫发预他事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304614_comment'></div>少卿去衡，君以衡人士多执经授业于其门者，不忍舍其师去，相率裒金买宅一区以家之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304614_comment'></div>余庚辰辛巳入潭幕，于衡为近，一时台府，如俞公徵、赵公善践、孙公得舆、李公东，皆持节与梅叔交，争馆粲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304614_comment'></div>余每欲沿檄游石鼓，与君瀹泉煮茗，相叩击，不能得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304614_comment'></div>君亦欲至潭访余，而诸公之在衡者恐其为有力者夺去，竟不与行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304614_comment'></div>壬午春，余以忧归，声问不相接者十有八年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304614_comment'></div>己亥夏，有以衰绖造吾门，视其刺不知为何来，使介者诘之，知其为梅叔之子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304614_comment'></div>亟出迎之，坐定，且泣且言曰：「棐不夭，先君家衡三十六年，壬辰归故里，葺先庐为终焉计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304614_comment'></div>不幸戊戌之闰月下世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304614_comment'></div>葬且有日，棐哀先志不就，大惧岁月久且沉泯，无取證于来世，求夫子之文刻墓石以传，则先君为不朽矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304614_comment'></div>于是系其谱而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304614_comment'></div>方氏自光之固始来，十有四代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304614_comment'></div>祖金紫公庭范，宰长乐，治产于莆，遂为莆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304614_comment'></div>君大父有为、父冲卿，潜德弗耀，母林氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304614_comment'></div>君生而岐嶷，家贫无书，借于邻族，一目数行俱下，终身不遗忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304614_comment'></div>长为诸公要人客，所为文操笔立就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304614_comment'></div>世有业进士不习为外学，至目之为屠龙无用之技，亦有专攻诗词骈俪而不屑作原夫辈语，以是为童子雕虫，壮夫耻之者，惟梅叔兼其所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304614_comment'></div>故自少至老，挟耿耿者以游四方，而岁得子弟束修，及青云贵人馈遗以自肥其遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304614_comment'></div>家衡日，买姬妾数十人，吹笙鼓琴，歌舞以娱宾客，感时抚物，念家怀土，酒酣作乐府付歌者，清婉可爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304614_comment'></div>暨返故居，出所贮蓄，市田园以供粢盛，得视中人之产且过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304614_comment'></div>每语子棐曰：「吾辞家出游，时无半菽之畴，无卓锥之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1304614_comment'></div>今有田若干、屋若干，非有俸禄以置之，田吾笔耕之田，屋吾书中之屋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1304614_comment'></div>虽然，吾岂为吾身及汝曹温饱计哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1304614_comment'></div>吾少读书，有志当世，谓得百里为之宰，必求如卓密令、鲁中牟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1304614_comment'></div>得千里为之牧，必求如田仁会、元结辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1304614_comment'></div>今无能以尺寸及物，岂吾志不如古人，吾才不及今人耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1304614_comment'></div>是有命焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1304614_comment'></div>吾固安之矣，力学成吾志，汝曹勉之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1304614_comment'></div>棐诵其言以告，余为愀然叹曰：士所植立系其志，所逢合系其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1304614_comment'></div>今窃科进身有贪婪苟贱者，官日大，流毒于民日深，橐金与屋数世不肖子孙用不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1304614_comment'></div>乃使志士仁人以济人利物为心，不得施设万一分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1304614_comment'></div>使之卖文为活，仅得数亩田数椽屋，以庥寿其后嗣，则自诡以为诗书之末效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1304614_comment'></div>至于身不得行其志，且以望其子若孙焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1304614_comment'></div>吁，是可悲也已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1304614_comment'></div>君讳应龙，以字行于世，晚以梅窗居士自命，享年六十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1304614_comment'></div>娶吴，继赵，先卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1304614_comment'></div>男一人，即吾友棐也，为吾族乙未特魁之侄婿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1304614_comment'></div>孙四：曰炳，曰焕，曰炜，曰烨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1304614_comment'></div>女二：长适营道宰商景春，次适进士陈伯顺，早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1304614_comment'></div>棐以己亥九月六日壬申领诸孙奉君柩葬于兴化县广业里牛冈之竹峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1304614_comment'></div>昔君在衡日谒术者，得卦兆有「牛冈寻吉穴，归葬竹峰前」之句，今所葬之地之名与兆协，岂天閟神藏以厚吉人，他日将有兴者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1304614_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1304614'>族望兮堂堂，声名兮洸洸，走四方兮皇皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1304614_comment'></div>不贵不寿兮返故乡，从龟从筮兮归吉藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1304614_comment'></div>不在其身在于其子孙兮，吾为之责报于苍苍。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1304614_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年</a>　复官通判赣州，未到任。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='749ef194f9e74541b49b0fb6e33fc1f8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("749ef194f9e74541b49b0fb6e33fc1f8");'><span id='749ef194f9e74541b49b0fb6e33fc1f8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1248')">1248年</a>，65岁</div><div id='749ef194f9e74541b49b0fb6e33fc1f8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1248')">1248年3月4日</a>　居乡奉祠。三月四日卒。除司农少卿，积阶朝请郎。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='abf9f58b414c40d6a90a0a30f0cab8ad_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("abf9f58b414c40d6a90a0a30f0cab8ad");'><span id='abf9f58b414c40d6a90a0a30f0cab8ad_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1216&endYear=1217')">1216-1217年</a>，33-34岁</div><div id='abf9f58b414c40d6a90a0a30f0cab8ad' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1216&endYear=1216')">1216年</a>　冬，入京应试。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1217&endYear=1217')">1217年5月8日</a>　廷对策，直陈内忧外患。作品：《丁丑廷对策》<div id='poem_1304552' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304552' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304552?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丁丑廷对策</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉定十年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304552")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304552_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304552'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304552'>臣对：臣闻治道无穷，本之圣经则愈求而愈有；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304552_comment'></div>圣学不息，施之圣治则愈久而愈新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304552_comment'></div>盖圣经非小用，皆所以示万世帝王出治之规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304552_comment'></div>圣学非具文，必有以得隆古帝王求治之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304552_comment'></div>终身求治，于学无得，是之谓不知本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304552_comment'></div>究心于学，而不及见之设施，是之谓不知用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304552_comment'></div>必其学日进于一日，而其治日新于一日，然后可以无负于圣经也矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304552_comment'></div>臣恭惟皇帝陛下图维政治之久，更阅义理之多，日御经筵，讲学不辍，咨访儒臣，切问有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304552_comment'></div>兹复延见四方韦布之士，赐之清问，俾之穷圣经之奥，明人道之务，竟其条贯以为对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304552_comment'></div>臣诚不佞，窃谓陛下前此凡五策士矣，皆未尝援经以为问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304552_comment'></div>今兹之策，其诸有见于治道之真不可以无所本欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304552_comment'></div>以陛下圣学高明，而犹屈己延问如此其切，臣有以窥陛下平日之学，不徒求之章句，必欲见之政治，今日之问，不徒责之以空言，必欲因言以求用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304552_comment'></div>臣一介浅学，生长明时，固尝涉圣经之涯涘，而未究其渊源，何足以称塞圣问？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304552_comment'></div>然尝闻其略矣，请先以历代帝王之所以学者为陛下诵言之，而后条陈圣策之所及者，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304552_comment'></div>臣闻五帝有心学，三王有家学，汉、唐之君有诸儒讲说之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304552_comment'></div>循汉、唐讲说之名，而得帝王心传、家传之实者，其惟祖宗盛时乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304552_comment'></div>夫有五帝之学则有五帝之治，有三王之学则有三王之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304552_comment'></div>学止于诸儒之讲说，故其治亦止于汉、唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304552_comment'></div>而祖宗之治所以高跨帝王，俯视秦、汉者，以其有经筵讲说之勤，而兼有得于心学、家学之懿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304552_comment'></div>昔者文籍未生，典谟未作，所学者何书？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304552_comment'></div>广成君畴之徒无所规寻其声光，所与从学者何人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304552_comment'></div>但见夫危微精一，文字不立，都俞吁咈，训说不形，信乎为五帝之心学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304552_comment'></div>商之高宗自监于先王成宪之外无馀学，周之成王自率由旧章之外无馀学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304552_comment'></div>彼其故家文献，有所谓圣谟之彰、方册之布者，皆其平日之所服习而力行，信乎其为三王之家学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304552_comment'></div>更汉历唐，好学之君先后相望，讲学之臣代不乏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1304552_comment'></div>然而心学无本，家学无传，则亦徒自弊于言语文字而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1304552_comment'></div>故刺经以作王制，非不知学也，而黄老清净之习得以汩之，故文帝之治知富而不知教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1304552_comment'></div>诏诸儒论五经同异，非不知学也，而杂霸刑名之术有以锢之，故宣帝之治见刑而不见德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1304552_comment'></div>以锐情经术之君而躬行仁义之不终，以《无逸》为图之世而改为山水以自逸，则虽石渠、白虎之开，宏文、集贤之置，祗见其地之为文具耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1304552_comment'></div>虽广厦细旃之讲，前师后儒之延，但见其官之为具员耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1304552_comment'></div>学无得于心传、家传之妙，而仅止于讲说之美观，此其治所以止于汉、唐欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1304552_comment'></div>恭惟祖宗列圣相承，以正心诚意为学之本原，以尊守家法为学之纲领，以儒臣讲读为朋友切磋之益，以宫庭隐奥为暗室不欺之地，故观《舜典》而叹后世刑网之密，讲《泰》卦而知君臣相通之情，得九经之旨于《记》之《中庸》，悟九族之亲于《诗》之《角弓》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1304552_comment'></div>所以贻谋燕翼者此学，而所以纂承绍述者亦此学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1304552_comment'></div>所以为百圣继绝统者此学，而所以为生灵开太平者亦此学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1304552_comment'></div>是以宏模懿范，醲政美化，辉奕帝王之上，有非汉、唐中主之所敢望者，岂非祖宗之学得之于心传、家传之妙，而不止于汉、唐讲说之故事欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1304552_comment'></div>今陛下之学，祖宗之学也，而陛下之治犹有愧于祖宗之治，是诚天下之所共疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1304552_comment'></div>此臣未敢以今日圣学之新为陛下喜，而必以他日圣治之新为陛下望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1304552_comment'></div>臣谨昧死上愚对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1304552_comment'></div>臣伏读圣策曰：「朕以寡昧，获承祖宗之绪，宵衣旰食，临政愿治，二纪于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1304552_comment'></div>固尝延进多士，冀闻谠言，未尝不虚己以听，志勤道远，每怀惕若」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1304552_comment'></div>臣有以见陛下思致理之惟艰，而知求言之有益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1304552_comment'></div>臣闻人主之德与天同运，不可无刚健不息之诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1304552_comment'></div>人主之治与日俱新，不可无奋发必为之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1304552_comment'></div>陛下愿治之心不为不切，而竟未有以副陛下之愿者，意者新天下之机在陛下未知所以运乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1304552_comment'></div>有复夏配天之志，则虽一成之旅，可以新一夏于纪纲既乱之馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1304552_comment'></div>有内修外攘之心，则虽十乘之戎，可以新一周于《小雅》尽废之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1304552_comment'></div>乌有堂堂天下，而不思所以作而新之者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1304552_comment'></div>乃者恭闻经筵讲读，圣意有悟于仁明英武之旨，而曰武乃断决之谓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1304552_comment'></div>陛下之所谓断决，即臣之所谓作新者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1304552_comment'></div>而臣之至愚极陋，犹必以日新之治为陛下勉者，非欲陛下一切更张以激天下之多事，非欲陛下专意慧察以摇天下之大本也，亦惟愿陛下先明朝廷之意向，先定士大夫之议论而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1304552_comment'></div>盖朝廷之意向不明，不足以新天下之精神；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1304552_comment'></div>士大夫之议论不一，不足以新天下之耳目，此臣之所甚忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1304552_comment'></div>朝廷之意向，天下之所趋也，今朝廷之意不达于士夫，士夫之意不白于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1304552_comment'></div>使其意果在于坚定欤，则当以谢安、王导镇抚江左之意明示天下，使之为安静之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1304552_comment'></div>使其意专在于振作欤，则当以勾践、种、蠡奋发复雠之意明示天下，使之为兴复之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1304552_comment'></div>夫何狃于畏事者，不量时势之逆顺，而有惩创太过之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1304552_comment'></div>喜于生事者，不揣根本之强弱，而有轻举直前之快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1304552_comment'></div>无心于国，固安于废放而不屑为，一有志焉，又茫然不知上意之所向，而无以为用力之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1304552_comment'></div>此意向不明，臣知其不足以作新天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1304552_comment'></div>士大夫之议论，国是之所从出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1304552_comment'></div>今上之揆谋献策，则谓莫若谨守格法与天下相安于尺度之中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1304552_comment'></div>下之游谈聚议，则谓莫若削破绳墨，与天下相从于边幅之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1304552_comment'></div>尚儒术者缓不及事，主吏议者轻而寡谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1304552_comment'></div>持刑者曰吾知有国宪尔，虽微损忠厚之意，庸何伤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1304552_comment'></div>征利者曰吾知有国计尔，虽小戾仁义之说，夫何恤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1304552_comment'></div>一遗敌之币，或曰予之便，或曰拒之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1304552_comment'></div>一流民之归，或曰受之是，或曰却之是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1304552_comment'></div>其始纷纷，殆类筑室道旁之哗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1304552_comment'></div>其终悠悠，谁当发言盈庭之咎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1304552_comment'></div>故人心之既协者，或惑以异议而摇动；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1304552_comment'></div>物议之未允者，不参以正理而改图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1304552_comment'></div>此议论不一，臣知其不足以作新天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1304552_comment'></div>意向既不明白，议论又不纯一，陛下虽屡求谠言，臣未见其言之有益于治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1304552_comment'></div>虽每有志勤道远之叹，则但见其玩岁愒日而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1304552_comment'></div>臣愿陛下以日新求学之心而施之治者，亦必日日新又日新，如陛下之学焉，则天下之治可以符圣意之所期矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1304552_comment'></div>臣伏读圣策曰：「间者日御经幄，延访儒臣，相与讲论切磋，朝夕靡怠，益信夫六经之道穷之而益深，测之而益远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1304552_comment'></div>子大夫以儒术策名，咸造在庭，其有以推明大义，使朕措之天下国家，不亦休乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1304552_comment'></div>臣有以见陛下欲按经以求治，且俾臣等各援经以为对也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1304552_comment'></div>臣闻治之不可以不新，其来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1304552_comment'></div>六经之书，帝王出治之本也，而求其大要，亦不能外作新之一说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1304552_comment'></div>夫「周虽旧邦，其命维新」，则《诗》之所谓新也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1304552_comment'></div>「刚健笃实辉光，日新其德」，则《易》之所谓新也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1304552_comment'></div>《康诰》曰「作新民」，《书》亦以新为言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1304552_comment'></div>汤之《盘铭》曰「苟日新」，《记》亦以新为言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1304552_comment'></div>《周官》布政于正月，一年之新也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1304552_comment'></div>《春秋》系事于元年，一国之新也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1304552_comment'></div>陛下日与儒臣切磋讲论，亦尝及此否乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1304552_comment'></div>人主之学与经生学士异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1304552_comment'></div>求训诂之隐微，泥文辞之同异，此经生学士之学也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1304552_comment'></div>求之圣经之已言，质之古人之已行，举而措之天下之事业，此人主之学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1304552_comment'></div>臣伏草茅之中，窃闻陛下莅政之次年，奸臣擅朝，阴劝陛下临朝渊默，法天不言者十有三年，一旦天开圣衷，翻然改图，又十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1304552_comment'></div>比日以来，天日开明，睿号涣发，每于经筵间得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1304552_comment'></div>如论治道有体，则有用贤委任之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1304552_comment'></div>论谏官言事，则有明目达聪之训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1304552_comment'></div>论用人，则知君子小人之当辨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1304552_comment'></div>论用兵，则知师从中覆之非宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1304552_comment'></div>尧言之大，布在天下，不一而足，是圣学之新盖月异而岁不同矣，而圣治之日新，未能如圣学之日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1304552_comment'></div>故臣愿陛下自今以始，或于讲读之暇，或于延对之顷，俾儒臣于经学之中䌷绎古人作新天下之大义，朝思而夕惟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1304552_comment'></div>其理甚明，何穷之深，其效甚近，何测之远，则以此作新一意，措之天下国家，如运之掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1304552_comment'></div>臣之所以推明者，外此亦无馀义矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1304552_comment'></div>臣伏读圣策：「昔者六经之书，作于天纵之圣，皆所以统天地之心而垂万世之法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1304552_comment'></div>名虽有六，义实同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1304552_comment'></div>今观《经解》所谓入其国而可知者，其教亦有不同耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1304552_comment'></div>岂因其才而教亦异耶，抑教之固有次序耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1304552_comment'></div>后世儒者益之以《周官》，亦古义耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1304552_comment'></div>臣有以见陛下欲求六经理义之指归，而考订《经解》、《周官》之同异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1304552_comment'></div>臣闻夫子之作六经，百世以俟圣人而不惑者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1304552_comment'></div>《易》以发三才之蕴，幽而明之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1304552_comment'></div>《诗》以达上下之情，宣而导之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1304552_comment'></div>《礼》不止以升降揖逊之文纪之也，教民之中者在焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1304552_comment'></div>《乐》不止以铿锵节奏之末为之也，教民之和者在焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1304552_comment'></div>《书》以述盛世之事而系之以秦、鲁者，不绝后世之为帝王也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1304552_comment'></div>《春秋》以纪衰世之变而终之以获麟者，犹冀世变之可以或变返也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1304552_comment'></div>夫子之道不行于当世，而悯当世之大坏极弊，急欲扶持而安全之，其心至拳拳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1304552_comment'></div>故每至其邦，必闻其政焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1304552_comment'></div>每见其人，必观其教焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1304552_comment'></div>见其洁静精微疏通知远，则知其为《易》《书》之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1304552_comment'></div>见其广博易良敦厚温柔，则知其为《诗》《乐》之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1304552_comment'></div>见其属辞比事，则知其为《春秋》之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1304552_comment'></div>夫子之教，如春风时雨之于物，随其限量，各使之足其所欲焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1304552_comment'></div>故其道之大，虽天下莫之能容，而人心秉彝之不泯，当时之人已有日用而不自知者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1304552_comment'></div>其后汉儒得《周官》一书，从而附之，使礼乐之文为制度，万世而下，与先王建立民极之意相为流通而无间断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1304552_comment'></div>此其忧世之心，虽夫子不得而绝之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1304552_comment'></div>后之人主苟得而用之，则夫子之愿毕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1304552_comment'></div>臣观祖宗盛时，六经之学光明盛大，昭昭乎若揭日月而行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1304552_comment'></div>中兴以后尤切，崇高道德性命之书，家传而人诵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1304552_comment'></div>曩者权臣用事，排斥正人，鄙薄正学，党以消节义之气，伪以污修洁之儒，教道不立，人心不正，天下之学士盖切齿之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1304552_comment'></div>爰自更化以来，首以崇教尊经为先务，而圣策所及又发明而铺张之，天下方凛凛然有回心向道之望矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1304552_comment'></div>臣愿陛下日明此教，以迪人心，以化天下，则夫子作六经之本心亦如是而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1304552_comment'></div>臣伏读圣策曰：「朕观汉廷之间，率俾以经对，盖人道之务在是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1304552_comment'></div>方今之务多矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1304552_comment'></div>臣有以见陛下嘉尚汉儒之知经，而欲责臣等以世务之通达也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1304552_comment'></div>臣闻经学之在天下，本无时而泯灭，特在后之人用之如何耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1304552_comment'></div>汉之君臣相与讲究六经之义多矣，得之而善用者，自董仲舒援《春秋》对策之外，臣未见其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1304552_comment'></div>晁错之刑名、孙弘之变诈，在廷之策援经考古，非不深切著明，而人非正人，学非正学，陋乎无以议为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1304552_comment'></div>陛下慨念方今之事，必求圣经所载有关于人道之务者以策臣，臣请即圣问所及而条陈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1304552_comment'></div>《书》有「惟时惟几，敕天之命」之言，《诗》有「敬天之威，毋敢戏豫」之戒，《易》言体天行健，必本之夕惕之诚，《记》言国有休祥，必归之至诚之感，《周官》重冯相保章之职，《春秋》严日食地震之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1304552_comment'></div>陛下观之此，则知敬天之务矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1304552_comment'></div>《书》有「民惟邦本，本固邦宁」之训，《诗》有「民亦劳止，汔可小康」之讥，《易》言厚下深戒剥床而及肤，《记》言子民必欲时使而薄敛，《周官》有委积救荒之政，《春秋》惩城筑不时之非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1304552_comment'></div>陛下观之，此则知爱民之务矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1304552_comment'></div>利口之风必移于三纪之馀，民德之壹必基于有二之服，曰防淫则有政矣，曰奇邪则有禁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1304552_comment'></div>此经之言风俗不可以不厚者然也，陛下知之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1304552_comment'></div>有车服之庸，不可无明试之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1304552_comment'></div>有官爵之予，不可无论辨之素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1304552_comment'></div>风之自正而入变，由仁人之不遇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1304552_comment'></div>世之自泰而入否，由君子之道消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1304552_comment'></div>此经之言人才不可以不择者然也，陛下知之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1304552_comment'></div>胄子之教所以见虞廷之太和，鱼丽之备所以见周室之文物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1304552_comment'></div>观司徒大胥之典，则知世之所以盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1304552_comment'></div>观六羽楹桷之书，则知世之所以衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1304552_comment'></div>陛下傥欲礼乐之兴，观之经足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1304552_comment'></div>明王慎德，四夷咸宾，常德既修，武事可立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1304552_comment'></div>观《萃》卦之象，则知戎器当备于不虞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1304552_comment'></div>观纪侯之传，则知复雠实切于大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1304552_comment'></div>陛下傥欲疆圉之固，观之此足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1304552_comment'></div>虽然，此其大略也，惟陛下既以经为问，臣不得不以经对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1304552_comment'></div>若夫圣策所及六条，臣当以实利害言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1304552_comment'></div>臣伏读圣策曰：「朕严恭寅畏，将以格天意也，而灾沴未免于间作」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1304552_comment'></div>陛下之言及此，天意将格于陛下之一言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1304552_comment'></div>陛下自即位至今，灾异之变凡几见矣，郁攸煽灾，都城为甚，星纬失次，占史屡书，旱蝗相仍，日月薄蚀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1304552_comment'></div>今岁之春，沙雾塞天，四阳之月，坤载震动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1304552_comment'></div>天之警告陛下者，乃所以仁爱陛下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1304552_comment'></div>陛下虽忧勤畏天，而未能弭天变者，政事之设施未能皆当于天心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1304552_comment'></div>宫闱之中，横赐时及于罔功，非天命有德矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1304552_comment'></div>辇毂之下，犴狱且至于失入，非天讨有罪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1304552_comment'></div>东南之民力已竭，而未有一分之宽，岂惟天惠民之意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1304552_comment'></div>中原之民望方切，而未慰箪壶之望，岂福夏祸夷之道乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1304552_comment'></div>而最可议者，陛下有忧勤之实，群臣多容悦之谀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1304552_comment'></div>遇旱蝗则曰蝗不为灾，睹星变则曰应在他分，苏湖小熟盛称有年，闽广饥荒掩讳不奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1304552_comment'></div>以四方水旱盗贼之变，屡警君心者何人，以阴阳不和咎在臣等者何人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1304552_comment'></div>陛下往岁大享明堂，熙事告成，群臣作赞美之诗，陛下深念旱伤之馀，却而不受，陛下之谦德如此，在廷之臣其有惭色否乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1304552_comment'></div>臣愿陛下益坚严恭寅畏之诚，勿信谗谄面谀之说，行此诚意而日新之，则天变弭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1304552_comment'></div>臣伏读圣策曰：「惠养赒恤所以厚民生也，而愁叹犹见其未苏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1304552_comment'></div>陛下之念及此，民心将感于陛下之一念矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1304552_comment'></div>陛下自即位至今，民生多艰，阅之熟矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1304552_comment'></div>淮民死兵，浙民死岁，湖广之民死盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1304552_comment'></div>以京畿而言，则一间湫隘而数家居之，一夫经营而数口仰之，皇皇乎一饱之无期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1304552_comment'></div>以外郡而言，乐岁之禾场甫筑，而巨室并之，凶年之四壁赤立，而横敛困之，凛凛乎朝夕之不相保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1304552_comment'></div>民之所以不忍叛贰者，以陛下之仁心仁闻素有以结之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1304552_comment'></div>陛下有尧、舜之仁而民不被其泽者，陛下之吏不肖，不足以广宣德意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1304552_comment'></div>内藏坊场之钱，积十馀年经赦不与原免，民之怨愤无愬者，十室而三四焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1304552_comment'></div>此在京之民可念也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1304552_comment'></div>两浙和买之绢，昔数五端，今增而为十，民之逃亡求避者，十室而五六焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1304552_comment'></div>此两浙之民可念也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1304552_comment'></div>淮甸丁钱之扰，民不安于土著矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1304552_comment'></div>广右和籴之扰，民不足于积仓矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1304552_comment'></div>一变盐钞，行二八、三七之令，海濒无巨商矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1304552_comment'></div>一行新楮，有估籍未还之家，通都无富室矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1304552_comment'></div>往往官吏知盈车受俸之可乐，而不知野有饿莩之可哀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1304552_comment'></div>知一家向隅之可忧，而不知一路向隅之可念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1304552_comment'></div>陛下往岁一遇大旱，尝有内宴却而不御，曰：「百姓不得饭，吾何有于酒」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1304552_comment'></div>陛下仁言入人如此，不知若官吏者亦闻之否乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1304552_comment'></div>臣愿陛下亟取民之蟊贼者痛惩而力去之，使之不得久其恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1304552_comment'></div>行此仁政而日新之，则民瘼苏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1304552_comment'></div>臣伏读圣策曰：「躬行以帅下，而民风之未醇」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1304552_comment'></div>臣谓陛下之俭德有素而民未化者，陛下未知所以新天下之民俗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1304552_comment'></div>盖风俗之淳漓，原于法制之修废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1304552_comment'></div>今天下之风俗侈矣，宫室高华，僭侈无度，昔尝禁矣，今僭儗之习，连甍而相望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1304552_comment'></div>销金翠羽，蠹耗不赀，昔又尝戢之矣，今销毁之家列肆而争利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1304552_comment'></div>士夫一饮之费，至糜十金之产，不惟素官为之，而初仕亦效其尤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1304552_comment'></div>妇女饰簪之微，至当十万之直，不惟巨室为之，而中产亦强仿之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1304552_comment'></div>后宫朝有服饰，夕行之于民间矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1304552_comment'></div>上方昨有制造，明布之于京师矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1304552_comment'></div>臣恐此风骎骎不已，则倡优后饰之侈，必蹈后元之风，而过朝自易车服，将无如绛、商之习于法者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1304552_comment'></div>臣愿陛下明诏有司，申法制以为之禁，则旧染污俗咸与惟新，不独见于仲康之时矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1304552_comment'></div>臣伏读圣策曰：「简拔以用材，而吏治之未振」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1304552_comment'></div>臣谓陛下之作成有道，而吏未得人者，陛下未知所以新天下之人才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1304552_comment'></div>盖人才之贤否关于心术之邪正，今士大夫心术之坏，胚胎于进身之苟贱，养成于居官之苟容，败露于临难之苟免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1304552_comment'></div>积是三坏，心术之正无几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1304552_comment'></div>方为小吏，无心远器，以贿为缔交之媒，以货为生死之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1304552_comment'></div>一齿朝绅，顾惜愈重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1304552_comment'></div>人知其邪正也，不敢言于眷宠方隆之初，而必言于势位已去之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1304552_comment'></div>政知其得失也，不敢辩于意旨未露之先，而必言于趋舍已判之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1304552_comment'></div>向者西蜀之变，抗义而死者，尚见于闾巷之细夫、闺门之女子，而搢绅大夫能守死而不变者，百仅一二焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1304552_comment'></div>是何甘为臭秽之生，而不愿为芬芳之死如此也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1304552_comment'></div>比日以来，诺诺者盈庭而谔谔者卷舌，容容者接武而皎皎者遁形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1304552_comment'></div>臣恐此风滋蔓日极，将有如贾谊所谓主上有患则立而观之者，而求其如令尹子文自毁其家以纾楚国之难者，曾几何人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1304552_comment'></div>臣愿陛下明诏大臣，于用人之际，必察其心术之微以为用舍，则新美天下之士，周宣王不得专美于前矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1304552_comment'></div>圣策曰：「举偏补弊而阙政尚多，何敢言礼乐之兴」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1304552_comment'></div>臣伏读至此，窃见陛下之有志于远者大者，而为万世计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1304552_comment'></div>臣闻自古礼乐之兴，必基于百年积德之素，而庙堂道揆之任，乃制作之攸属也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1304552_comment'></div>以陛下求治之久，礼乐可兴而未兴者，簿书期会之细务有以弊之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1304552_comment'></div>今论道经邦之地，当存朝廷之大体可也，夫何郡国应有细务，必皆取朝廷施行？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1304552_comment'></div>中书坐堂涉笔而书者此事也，启印而行者亦此事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1304552_comment'></div>文书填委，相府有甚于他司矣，朝廷应有除擢，不问部阙与夫堂除，悉关白于庙堂而后敢与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1304552_comment'></div>光范之门，今日所见宾客者差除也，明日所入格状者亦差除也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1304552_comment'></div>衣冠如市，相府尤甚于铨曹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1304552_comment'></div>究心于小则大者必遗，计功于近则远图或缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1304552_comment'></div>终日经理百务，力且不给，何暇及于定民志之礼，移民风之乐，以为此迂阔之事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1304552_comment'></div>昔王吉谓汉之公卿遭遇其时，不知明礼乐定王制，以建万世之策，而溺于俗吏之细务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1304552_comment'></div>房玄龄日阅讼牒，以烦碎自累，一旦乃浃背于礼乐之问，此后之为人臣者所当戒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1304552_comment'></div>今陛下必欲兴礼乐，则自今以始，必清中书之务，亟图其远者、大者，王道一盛，礼乐其有不兴乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1304552_comment'></div>此亦作新天下之大务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1304552_comment'></div>圣策曰：「选将练兵，而武事未立，何以成疆圉之固」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1304552_comment'></div>臣伏读至此，若有以激愚忠之欲言者，敢详以对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1304552_comment'></div>臣谓文治有馀而武功不竞，内治未举而外圉莫安，莫今日为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1304552_comment'></div>选将练兵，苟切于陛下之焦劳，则天下之事可为矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1304552_comment'></div>陛下其亦知今日无可用之将乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1304552_comment'></div>臣闻有择将之道，有任将之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1304552_comment'></div>以今日择将言之，陛下尝诏大臣各举将才以闻矣，然介胄之士非无过人之才，而伏于营垒符籍之中，罕与搢绅接，故知其才者实难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1304552_comment'></div>加之军将之间转相忌刻，又多方以困辱之，使其才不足以自见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1304552_comment'></div>岂营垒符籍之中，果无人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1304552_comment'></div>昔者祖宗盛时，求之于偏校之中，可以得岳飞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1304552_comment'></div>求之于敢勇之中，可以得韩世忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1304552_comment'></div>臣愿陛下布擢卒为将之令于军中，则将才出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1304552_comment'></div>以今之任将言之，讲解以来，向之立功阃外者无端而置之于閒散，若曰天下可常无事，焉用此曹为也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1304552_comment'></div>比者羽檄一驰，仓皇四顾，乃下一纸以示其有收用之渐，臣恐不足以尽得其心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1304552_comment'></div>昔唐郭子仪之为将也，以鱼朝恩之谮，既夺之兵柄矣，及光弼败河朔，则又召之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1304552_comment'></div>程元振忌言一入，既罢其节度矣，及回纥入寇，则又召之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1304552_comment'></div>无事则麾之而去，有事则招之而来，子仪赤心为国，初不较其或用或舍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1304552_comment'></div>今之为将者，乌得人人如子仪哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1304552_comment'></div>臣愿陛下委之以诚，畀之以权，用之则勿疑，疑之则勿用，则任将得其道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1304552_comment'></div>陛下亦知今无可仗之兵乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1304552_comment'></div>臣闻兵数不可以不多，兵心尤不可以不固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1304552_comment'></div>以今之兵数言之则不多矣，大军折阅，武定归农，摧锋、飞虎半歼于敌，骁骑健将去而为盗，禁卫之卒不盈十万，九江、池阳驻劄之额仅万三千有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1304552_comment'></div>臣恐缓急之际，首尾寡援，必至于两军以马少为辞，不复出塞，六军皆驱市人而战，不能受甲矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1304552_comment'></div>以今之兵心言之，则不固矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1304552_comment'></div>向者所募之卒放归田里，而怨气未消，后来军功之滥，多方沮抑，而锐气日铄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1304552_comment'></div>加之主帅非人，苦于掊剋，数杂恶之物而配之，名曰乾利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1304552_comment'></div>乘工造之时而勒之，名曰陪陌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1304552_comment'></div>房廊贴陌之钱、八厢常例之目，日增月益而未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1304552_comment'></div>臣恐兵贫既甚，变生不虞，必至于泾原戍卒以粝食而召乱，关内禁兵以乏粮而叫呼矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1304552_comment'></div>臣愿陛下明敕边郡，下招募土兵之令，而厚为之赏，以足其数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1304552_comment'></div>戒饬主帅，无袭掊剋之弊，而严为之罚，以结其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1304552_comment'></div>如是，则将既得人，兵又可用，而犹以武事未立，守圉未固为忧，臣未之信也，亦在陛下作新兵将而用之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1304552_comment'></div>臣伏读圣策曰：「伊欲嘉祥降于上，德泽流于下，教化行而习俗美，法度修而众职举，纳天下于中和而措外内于无患，庶几治古之盛，无愧载籍之传，果何道以臻此」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1304552_comment'></div>臣谓陛下始之所以策臣者及于圣经之可用，终之所以策臣者及于时政之实用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1304552_comment'></div>臣惟愿陛下日新之治，常如日新之学，则德泽既及于民，何患休祥之不降于天？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1304552_comment'></div>惟新之命，臣知其未艾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1304552_comment'></div>职守既修于士大夫，风俗自美于天下，陶然日新之政，臣知其有期也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1304552_comment'></div>陛下新之一日，则有一日之功，新之一岁，则有一岁之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1304552_comment'></div>中和之教一成，内外之患自弭，古治之盛，岂止庶几载籍之传？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1304552_comment'></div>何但无愧，抑犹未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1304552_comment'></div>以言其在内之事势，则纪纲虽张，有弛之萌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1304552_comment'></div>公论虽伸，有屈之渐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1304552_comment'></div>人心暂合而易离，倖门已窒而复启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1304552_comment'></div>以言其在外之事势，则窃生事之戒，以盖其畏事之愆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1304552_comment'></div>假安静之名，以便其茍安之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1304552_comment'></div>雨且至矣，而彻桑之备未修；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1304552_comment'></div>火且然矣，而积薪之寝未悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1304552_comment'></div>以巍巍之中国，常若过于有所畏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1304552_comment'></div>以悠悠之岁月，常若安于不敢为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1304552_comment'></div>则微臣之忧，盖未歇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1304552_comment'></div>陛下所以策臣者至矣，而犹丁宁申训之曰：「子大夫明先圣之学，按经考古，必有至当之论，其为朕推求其本，科别其条，使悉见之于行事，而不徒驰骛乎空言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1304552_comment'></div>熟之究之，详著于篇，朕将亲览」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1304552_comment'></div>臣之底蕴亦粗罄于前矣，至此伏而思之，以为求言于多事之时，不可与平居无事之时同，则献言于不讳之朝，亦当竭其忠赤而无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1304552_comment'></div>臣闻外裔之盛衰，本无关于中国之大势，而吾国之政事，不可无远大之图维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1304552_comment'></div>盖善医疾者不忧风寒之为患，而惟忧元气之不充；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1304552_comment'></div>善医国者不忧疆埸之多虞，而惟忧朝廷之有弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1304552_comment'></div>臣请借汉以为谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1304552_comment'></div>汉自宣帝以前，匈奴之患无日无之，今年入云中，明年入上郡，而汉日以治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1304552_comment'></div>至中世而后，某年单于来朝，某年斩某单于告郊庙，而汉治日以不振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1304552_comment'></div>夫外裔之强，无损于汉之治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1304552_comment'></div>外裔之弱，无救于汉之衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1304552_comment'></div>盖盛衰之势，在汉而不在外也明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1304552_comment'></div>汉之盛时，赏罚必明，号令必信，政事出于中书而无中制之患，集议达于博士而无偏信之失，所以治其国中之事者至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1304552_comment'></div>匈奴虽强，岂非疮癣之疾哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1304552_comment'></div>及其末也，舛政逆令，间见层出，天子养安而一身痛痒之不知，大臣养尊而社稷休戚之不恤，百官庶府委靡于下，宦官女子睥睨于旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1304552_comment'></div>是其中国之事盖日非矣，匈奴虽弱，何有于汉哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1304552_comment'></div>今敌势就衰，假息于汴，中原豪杰并起而亡之，人孰不以此为中国贺？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1304552_comment'></div>而臣区区之过计，惟愿陛下与二三大臣日治其政事，日训其人民，监汉之所以得而戒其所以失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1304552_comment'></div>邻国之强弱，不足以易其勇怯之心，惟先治其在我者，一旦事机之至，则明中国之大义，定天下之大计，指日可俟矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1304552_comment'></div>此非臣之臆说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1304552_comment'></div>昔韩琦进言于仁宗曰：「元昊狂僭，必为边患，选将训兵，修甲营城，此外忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1304552_comment'></div>纪纲不立，忠佞不分，赏罚不明，号令不信，浮费靡节，颁赐不常，务宴逸之近游，纵宫庭之奢侈，受女谒之干请，容近昵之侥倖，此内忧也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1304552_comment'></div>臣观仁宗之时，西戎小丑，特边鄙之事耳，而琦之所忧在于朝廷之上、宫阃之间，忠臣远虑，一至于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1304552_comment'></div>伏惟陛下反观内省，吾之纪纲果立欤，忠佞果分欤，赏罚号令果已明信欤，浮费颁赐果已裁节欤，女谒近习果已深防而力杜之欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1304552_comment'></div>万一朝廷政事未能无过差，宫阃堤防未能无罅漏，陛下固不可不早为之虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1304552_comment'></div>臣来自远方，不识忌讳，惟恃以直言取士，不以直言弃之，有本朝之家法在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1304552_comment'></div>廷试在即，使远方之士得尽其言，亦是美事，有陛下之圣言在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1304552_comment'></div>是以空臆而竟言之，惟陛下裁择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1304552_comment'></div>臣昧死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1304552_comment'></div>臣谨对。</div><div id='poem_sentence_312_1304552_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1217&endYear=1217')">1217年5月8日</a>　擢甲科第四人，补从事郎、防团推判官。作品：《谢省试参详林员外启》《谢殿试编排官聂侍郎启》<div id='poem_1304391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢省试参详林员外启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1217年5月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304391")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304391'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304391'>升堂拜知己之恩，绨袍已敝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304391_comment'></div>入邸辱赠言之宠，华衮非荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304391_comment'></div>竦观挥洒之云烟，深惧取将于雷电。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304391_comment'></div>书绅起敬，藏笥为珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304391_comment'></div>窃以遇合之难，古今所叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304391_comment'></div>必大人君子，喜士素根于天性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304391_comment'></div>故后生晚进，委身愿出于门墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304391_comment'></div>况有如师生名位之绝严，鲜能略世俗礼文而相接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304391_comment'></div>必有卓荦不群之彦，方受特达殊常之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304391_comment'></div>如某者地寒无媒，天赋不腆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304391_comment'></div>少而有志，耻随馀子以浮沉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304391_comment'></div>壮不如人，安得名公之印可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304391_comment'></div>曩缘行役，得拜宗师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304391_comment'></div>出名骏之图，以华其归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304391_comment'></div>洒飞鸾之笔，以饰其陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304391_comment'></div>口共心语，愿托身炉鞴之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304391_comment'></div>人欲天从，果定价权衡之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304391_comment'></div>尝怀漫刺以晋谒，辄辱阍人之见辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304391_comment'></div>自蒙恩锡第以来，至束担言归之日，念不违函丈而径去，将归白庭闱以何辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304391_comment'></div>甫尔抠衣，便蒙倒屣，畀以名章之奖借，增其行色之光辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304391_comment'></div>得此于常人不足誇，受知于名世何其幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304391_comment'></div>昔韩昌黎送牛堪登第之序，至忘师道之尊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304391_comment'></div>苏东坡谢范公校文之书，或动乡人之喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304391_comment'></div>久无此事，今在我公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304391_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官前辈典刑，斯文宗匠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1304391_comment'></div>流落人间之述作，特泰山一毫芒之微；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1304391_comment'></div>提携天下之孤寒，有大厦千万间之庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1304391_comment'></div>致令么么，辱在品题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1304391_comment'></div>某敢不尊其所闻，勤乎未学？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1304391_comment'></div>文章末技，粗承交臂之传；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1304391_comment'></div>节义大闲，当励立身之戒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1304391_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1304393' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304393' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304393?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢殿试编排官聂侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1217年5月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304393")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304393_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304393'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304393'>数父执于慈恩之塔，稀若辰星；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304393_comment'></div>称门生于通德之乡，恍如霄汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304393_comment'></div>昔登堂不果，恐涉营私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304393_comment'></div>今假道遄归，将何辞谢？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304393_comment'></div>僭饬尺笺，仰呈丈席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304393_comment'></div>恭惟某官日未东即收于巍第，江以西莫著其大名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304393_comment'></div>诗社挥毫，妙思源泉之出地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304393_comment'></div>昕庭抗疏，精忠皦日之在天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304393_comment'></div>不由介绍而结主知，径躐清华而登从橐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304393_comment'></div>剸裁国用，鄙夷管、晏之近功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304393_comment'></div>经略中原，隘小孙刘之故画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304393_comment'></div>详审乎事机之会，更阅乎理义之多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304393_comment'></div>谓如根本之先强，则于恢拓也可待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304393_comment'></div>盖知彼而不知己，皆料敌之浅谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304393_comment'></div>必能发而又能收，乃济时之远略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304393_comment'></div>属北方之警未息，而西州之变复兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304393_comment'></div>人方忧蜀道之难，公往为雪山之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304393_comment'></div>至则事权之牵制，加之饥卒之跳梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304393_comment'></div>身持尺檄以直前，惟知死节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304393_comment'></div>神叱的卢之一跃，遂获生还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304393_comment'></div>浮言何伤乎日月之明，雅志已抗于烟霞之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304393_comment'></div>携诸郎于谢墅，会名胜于午桥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304393_comment'></div>耆英之会狄公，方春秋之未艾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304393_comment'></div>中国即相司马，宁朝暮之少淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304393_comment'></div>伏念某殖学代耕，卖文为活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1304393_comment'></div>元龙湖海之气，少也勃然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1304393_comment'></div>司马山川之游，今其倦矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1304393_comment'></div>为有阿㜷之养，漫从举子之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1304393_comment'></div>两玷乡书，一尘春榜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1304393_comment'></div>迨奉黄廷之对，空臆尽言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1304393_comment'></div>不知书生之疏，转喉触讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1304393_comment'></div>痛国论之未一，悯边衅之方开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1304393_comment'></div>惜诸将多陷谗言，乃援子仪之事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1304393_comment'></div>议宰相当存大体，恐贻王吉之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1304393_comment'></div>虽清朝许竭其愚衷，而时论或讥其太讦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1304393_comment'></div>发矢将穿于杨叶，及的辄差；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1304393_comment'></div>乘舟已迫于蓬莱，为风引去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1304393_comment'></div>向非借九鼎之力，当不止三筹之输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1304393_comment'></div>副本既不上于中书，贱刺亦羞通于光范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1304393_comment'></div>至谢知己，皆后众人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1304393_comment'></div>俯仰何心，升沉付分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1304393_comment'></div>谓今得斗粟之禄，可以无饥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1304393_comment'></div>岂不胜布衣之时，难乎一饱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1304393_comment'></div>兹迫瓜期之戍，方登荷橐之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1304393_comment'></div>如亮其今日之来，非为炙手；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1304393_comment'></div>当赐以片言之诲，庶使书绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1304393_comment'></div>此身已托大冶之中，他日冀轸遗簪之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1304393_comment'></div>但不负于素学，是谓报于异知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1304393_comment'></div>虽秃千毫，莫殚一感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1304393_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1304393_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='cc5951b07c54444b8a96b3b0b9b6192e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cc5951b07c54444b8a96b3b0b9b6192e");'><span id='cc5951b07c54444b8a96b3b0b9b6192e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1224&endYear=1229')">1224-1229年</a>，41-46岁</div><div id='cc5951b07c54444b8a96b3b0b9b6192e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1224&endYear=1224')">1224年</a>　秋，调浙西安抚司干办官。上启文拜见赵汝珰。作品：《谢赵漕启》<div id='poem_1304420' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304420' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304420?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赵漕启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1224年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304420")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304420_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304420'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304420'>父生师教之身，仆不轻于所托；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304420_comment'></div>德进言扬之选，公何取而见收？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304420_comment'></div>既不常亲炙于朝夕之间，又不能借助于左右之誉，惠出非望，始闻犹疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304420_comment'></div>乃以剪拂之过情，竟谓强毅而有立，玩诵至此，感慨久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304420_comment'></div>直道而行，寡与世合，中人以上，好与己同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304420_comment'></div>郑公良臣，尚恨义方有太直之操；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304420_comment'></div>曲江贤相，且嫌挺之负过劲之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304420_comment'></div>如某其人，何足比数？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304420_comment'></div>昔尝吐危言而对策，以讦见排；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304420_comment'></div>今复持直道以事人，似狂未醒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304420_comment'></div>斗升之禄，粗奉甘旨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304420_comment'></div>方寸之地，可质神明。<div class='inline'
