id='poem_sentence_43_1304386_comment'></div>子仪孤忠自许，但知国家有难则出身以当之，何暇与憸壬辈较曲直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1304386_comment'></div>然天下良将不多子仪也，则群小能夺帅权于反覆之顷者，尤不可不戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1304386_comment'></div>大抵君子立人之朝，其进以礼，退以义，如松柏之特立，如凤凰之孤鸣，断断乎无所依凭附丽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1304386_comment'></div>小人枉道以求合，苟有可以攀援者，疾趋而凑之，权臣用事则附权臣，妇寺有宠则附妇寺，近习得志则附近习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1304386_comment'></div>邪正之分各以其党，观人之法，概见于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1304386_comment'></div>臣观近日阉宦近习之徒得以毁誉臣下，荧惑主听，其名姓骎骎有闻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1304386_comment'></div>穴墉之狐不可灌也，伏社之鼠不可熏也，独不可于始入之涂而窒之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1304386_comment'></div>《易》有坚冰之戒，《诗》有桃虫之喻，陛下为贤人君子计，为社稷生灵计，不以臣位卑言高而亮其忠，则臣之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1304386_comment'></div>不然，苦语忤时，自掇罪戾而去，亦臣区区尽忠之职分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1304386_comment'></div>荐渎天威，惟陛下赦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1304386_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_1304386'>〔贴黄〕臣按熙宁初富弼为首相，尝献言曰：「执政大臣喜怒系人情之舒惨，邪正系朝廷之盛衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1304386_comment'></div>执政不和则有司不和，有司不和则万务不治，或分争于官府，或辩别于君前，咸蓄不平之心，举无至当之论」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1304386_comment'></div>此为执政不和言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1304386_comment'></div>今二相不合，臣愿申弼之言而敕戒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1304386_comment'></div>大臣协和，则贤和朝而物和野，天下之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1304386_comment'></div>臣又按秦王廷美以罪贬房陵，责咎忧悸，得以令终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1304386_comment'></div>太宗皇帝每念天伦，必悲泣不已，未踰三月立其子德恭，予之供赡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1304386_comment'></div>大臣宋琪谓此举舍过恤孤，足以感动天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1304386_comment'></div>比者奸臣以济邸葬于西溪泥淖之中，鬼如有知，必能为厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1304386_comment'></div>天怒民怨，职此之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1304386_comment'></div>欲乞圣慈恻然动心，命有司以礼改葬以妥其神，乃俟国本既定，然后为之立嗣，以释天怒，以弭民怨，非细故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1304386_comment'></div>臣第一劄首尾所言，信而有證，俱在国史，并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_65_1304386_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年闰7月</a>　因轮对直言得“狂生”名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年</a>　是年，有诗寄知漳州李韶。作品：《寄呈漳守李侍郎元善四首》<div id='poem_71188' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71188' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71188?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄呈漳守李侍郎元善四首<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1235年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_71188")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_71188_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_71188_0'>① 李韶自号竹湖，筠溪其祖也，尝守漳</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_71188'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71188'>棠木筠溪手自栽，竹湖又剖竹符来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71188'>祖孙相望风流盛，父老驩传春意回。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71188'>拔薤莫须施辣手，泛莲似更欠清才。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71188'>善人所至如甘雨，要洗漳民满面埃<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：余去漳未久，据所见言之。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71188'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_71188_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_71187' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71187' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71187?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1235年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_71187_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_71187'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71187'>侍郎佛地位中人，一饭何尝不念民。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71187_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71187'>泾渭同流须有别，雪霜杀物乃为仁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71187_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71187'>扬清可使贪夫愧，去恶能令善者伸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71187_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71187'>自笑狂生太饶舌，见诗少喜定多嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71187_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71187'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_71187_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_71313' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71313' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71313?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1235年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_71313_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_71313'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71313'>向来大姓虐穷闾，千亩农田浚作渠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71313'>黠吏鹰豪争攫肉，骄儿螂怒敢当车。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71313'>老丞嫉恶无容忍，直笔诛奸欲剪锄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71313'>解印此曹称快甚，惟民与士最愁予<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：骄儿谓李兰军。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71313'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_71313_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_71186' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71186' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71186?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1235年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_71186_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_71186'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71186'>陛前苦语犯龙鳞，朝退还遭丞相嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71186_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71186'>连削六阶为下吏，只饶一死与閒身。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71186_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71186'>命天所付须安分，贫士之常莫语人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71186_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71186'>惟有梅花无冷暖，玉堂茅舍一般春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71186_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71186'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_71186_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年</a>　在秘书省正字任上，上封事。作品：《丙申九月封事》<div id='poem_1304387' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304387' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304387?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙申九月封事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1236年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304387")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304387_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304387'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304387'>臣伏睹诏书，以季秋中辛明堂蒇事之夕，天大雨，雷非时发声，明威震怒，炳然甚著，令小大之臣，下至民庶，推原致灾之由，敷陈消变之策，凡朕躬过失，朝政缺违，悉意以言，靡有所讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304387_comment'></div>臣跪诵感泣，昧死进言：臣尝观先儒程颐论郊祀明堂之制，以为万物本乎天，人本乎祖，故于冬至为气之始，祭天而以祖配之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304387_comment'></div>万物成形于帝，人成形于父，故于季秋为物之成，享帝而以父配之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304387_comment'></div>盖古今制度不同，然郊尊而明堂亲，则未始不同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304387_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下季秋中辛有事明堂，圣祖神宗实与享之，而宁考在天之灵，则为犹亲，于列圣必其享祀之际，俨然若见其洋洋之神，忾然若闻其叹息之声也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304387_comment'></div>夫何衮冕方升，骏奔在列，牺牲未荐，盏笾未陈，而骤霪倾盆，黑潦满道，雷轰其响，电晔其光，圣心惕然，惧形玉色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304387_comment'></div>宰执而下，跼蹐颠沛，不得成礼而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304387_comment'></div>皇天之怒陛下，宁考之怒陛下也，至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304387_comment'></div>臣猥以狂愚，待罪丞郡，引领鸡赦，至于南陬，比之常年，罪缓旬日，臣诚爱君，诚忧国，朝夕危慄，食不下咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304387_comment'></div>肆赦既颁，惊魂甫定，越再信宿，复睹明纶，则知以明威震怒之故，广求臣庶之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304387_comment'></div>臣愚不肖，窃以为阴雨为沴，雷发非时，间亦有之，而独昭示于明禋之夕者，此皇天、宁考之积怒至是而后泄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304387_comment'></div>臣请为陛下言其获怒之端与夫解怒之道，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304387_comment'></div>陛下之身，皇天、宁考之所眷佑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304387_comment'></div>陛下能敬其身，乃所以敬天而敬宁考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304387_comment'></div>曲糵致疾，过于沉酣，妖冶伐性，深于陷溺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304387_comment'></div>中宫素以德选，有《小星》惠下之仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304387_comment'></div>妃嫔多以色进，有《绿衣》上僭之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304387_comment'></div>初秋踰旬，旷不视事，道路传播，人心忧疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304387_comment'></div>及莅正朝，宜远声色，嫔御异数，横出滋多，尤物为祟，不惟不芟夷之，又从而封殖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304387_comment'></div>在礼有云：子者亲之枝也，不敬其身，是伤其亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304387_comment'></div>陛下一身，十三圣责望之所归，千万世本支之所系，不知持觞席之戒，求所以养寿命之原，此皇天、宁考之所以怒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304387_comment'></div>陛下之位，皇天、宁考之所畀付也，陛下知天位之重，必知有以厚天叙之典，乃所以敬天而敬宁考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304387_comment'></div>故王何负于陛下，而使之魂魄之无依，岁时之绝祀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304387_comment'></div>弥远何功于陛下，而保全其富，可埒国家，简记其不学面墙之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304387_comment'></div>窃窥圣意，不过曰故王之在霅邸，有暧昧之过，故仇之也深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1304387_comment'></div>弥远之擅国命，有拥护之功，故德之也厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1304387_comment'></div>不思夫霅川告变，非出于故王之本心，天知之，宁考知之，陛下独不知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1304387_comment'></div>弥远专权，宜受贪天之酷罚，天厌之，宁考厌之，陛下独不厌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1304387_comment'></div>乱臣贼子何代无有，虽在本朝，亦所不免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1304387_comment'></div>远而京、黼，近而桧、侂，仅能窃弄威福，以毒臣下，未有敢行不义，戕贼人主之同气，如弥远之为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1304387_comment'></div>《诗》有《角弓》，为骨肉相怨而作也，乃以民之「胥然」、「胥效」为言，故王之冤未伸，弥远之罪未正，此皇天、宁考之所以怒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1304387_comment'></div>陛下自更化而后，立政用人当扫地以求更新，执政大臣当同心而捍王室，夫何庙堂造命之地，反有剑佩相攻之风？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1304387_comment'></div>朋左者则议右之机械深，党右者则诮左之门庭杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1304387_comment'></div>民讼在有司，而左之馆客乃以赂章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1304387_comment'></div>官职在朝廷，而右之族党乃以赃败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1304387_comment'></div>甚至浊夫黠子，久在台司，招权纳贿，犹如曩日金免昼攫而夜或暗投，鸡耻日攘而月犹未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1304387_comment'></div>司道揆者若罔闻知，但见榻前奏事，谬为恭逊，都堂当笔，公肆异同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1304387_comment'></div>盘石不任而栋倾，盐梅不和而鼎覆，庆历之车主于必行，元祐之舟戒其偏重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1304387_comment'></div>昔者君子协心为国，义同一家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1304387_comment'></div>今之大臣立党相倾，甚于仇敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1304387_comment'></div>天工之旷如此，而陛下方以代天理物望之，欲皇天、宁考之不怒，得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1304387_comment'></div>陛下自践阼以来，民之死于水火，死于旱荒，何可胜数？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1304387_comment'></div>金人殄灭，强敌方兴，机会虽来，事力未至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1304387_comment'></div>有妄男子抵掌谈兵，深入三京，尅日恢复，轻于一掷，折翅遄归，弃甲曳兵，只轮不返，粮食积贮，颗粒不留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1304387_comment'></div>边鄙之民残于斗战，暴骨如山；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1304387_comment'></div>内地之民困于转输，横尸塞道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1304387_comment'></div>国威由此损失，国用由此空虚，范、葵、子才之罪于是乎通天矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1304387_comment'></div>逆全送死，天实诛之，侥倖成功，执以要上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1304387_comment'></div>西蜀数州相继沦没，而巨镇如兴元，剿于戎马之一屯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1304387_comment'></div>京西八郡，莽为邱墟，而要害如襄阳，空于北军之一炬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1304387_comment'></div>宣和拓地，裔域乱华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1304387_comment'></div>开禧称兵，权臣函首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1304387_comment'></div>惟兵与民相依为生，兵端一开，民祸罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1304387_comment'></div>自宝庆以至于今，赤子之歼于干戈者，不知其几万亿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1304387_comment'></div>孝子仁人，以伐一木、杀一兽不以其时为非孝，岂有夭民之死如此其夥，而陛下方垂衣拱手以视之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1304387_comment'></div>欲皇天宁考之不怒，得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1304387_comment'></div>统有正传，尊无二上，人之母一，陛下之母三：荣邸则所出也，沂邸则所继也，寿明太后功冠高孟，则天下之母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1304387_comment'></div>方东朝无恙时，承颜顺色，凛如奉盈，彼二邸者安敢顾之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1304387_comment'></div>今宫室服御，竭力奉承，恩礼过隆，毋敢议者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1304387_comment'></div>濮园故实，载之瑶编，充类而言，礼可义起，何至权度不审，彼重此轻，以私灭公，以恩夺义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1304387_comment'></div>安知皇天、宁考之怒，不以外戚有用事之渐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1304387_comment'></div>自古妇寺，易生厉阶，陛下英明神武，如日在天，便嬖使令安敢预政？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1304387_comment'></div>问之朝野，具识姓名，何物巨珰，辄进淫巧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1304387_comment'></div>蕞尔近习，久怙私恩，贵艳妃嫱，辅车相依，能梯群小，能阱忠良，能间君臣，能乱嫡媵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1304387_comment'></div>思昔盛时，元老一语，立去守忠，宫中内降，深惮杜衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1304387_comment'></div>今朝无厚德重望可压服之，弱者畏谗，巧者买誉，穿社之鼠莫之敢熏，在墉之隼莫之敢射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1304387_comment'></div>长此不已，为衅叵量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1304387_comment'></div>安知皇天宁考之怒，不以宦官近习有挠政之萌乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1304387_comment'></div>臣之所言获怒之端者六，而解怒之道，莫切于陛下之身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1304387_comment'></div>臣尝爱欧阳修之言曰：「自古帝王虽号至尊，未尝独处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1304387_comment'></div>其出而居外，不止百官奏事而已，必有经生学士讲论燕闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1304387_comment'></div>其入而居内，不止宦官宫妾而已，必有太子问安侍膳，宗室子弟驩然相接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1304387_comment'></div>计其一日之中，未尝一时独处也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1304387_comment'></div>修为此言，盖以选立皇子为仁宗劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1304387_comment'></div>今愚臣之告陛下，亦如修之告仁宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1304387_comment'></div>诚使元良一立，国本一正，天性之爱油然而生，清明在躬，嗜欲日损，间有御幸，必精必专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1304387_comment'></div>上帝降祥，笃生圣嗣，则选立者归之旧邸，有祥符故事在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1304387_comment'></div>陛下何惮何疑，而不蚤及此也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1304387_comment'></div>明禋之五日，陛下用汉灾异劾三公故事，参之淳熙近比，中出一纸，罢免二相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1304387_comment'></div>譬之人子受父母之谴而不能堪，则迁怒于家相而逐之，即日出关之命，毋乃太匆匆乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1304387_comment'></div>古先哲王之用大臣，疑则勿用，用则勿疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1304387_comment'></div>群公先正立人之朝，道合则留，不合则去，清之当去久矣，见几而作，屡失于几，色斯举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1304387_comment'></div>何止于色，抽身不勇，君子惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1304387_comment'></div>行简以经筵留，果合于进退之义否乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1304387_comment'></div>廉耻节礼以待君子，故宁损其身，不受戮辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1304387_comment'></div>一介之士馆于公卿之门，辞色不顺，望望去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1304387_comment'></div>至于逐客之令已下而又留之，士苟为留则亦可贱矣，况大臣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1304387_comment'></div>贾谊所谓握重权大臣，而有奴隶无耻之心，惜其党无有以此告之，而嗜进谄夫冀其弃鹿而怀鼷，未免见弹而思炙，反从而怂恿之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1304387_comment'></div>弥远柄国二十七年，天下人望在数十公，或屏弃不用，或用而不尽其才，荏苒至今，彫零殆尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1304387_comment'></div>清之当轴，收召诸贤，聚之本朝，最后而德秀至，参预命下，疾病婴之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1304387_comment'></div>文宗「识卿不早」之叹，至形当馈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1304387_comment'></div>诗人「邦国殄瘁」之惜，中外所同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1304387_comment'></div>咨夔继亡，了翁又去，元夫钜人，稀若晨星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1304387_comment'></div>陛下既去二相，环顾在廷，无可当枋用者，乃以相印起与之于南海之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1304387_comment'></div>与之天下大老也，其如耄及且病，未必肯来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1304387_comment'></div>揆席久虚，事权不一，性之、鸣复畏首畏尾，更相推逊，中书之务壅遏不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1304387_comment'></div>陛下起视四海之内，风涛如此，今为何时，而可无济川作楫者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1304387_comment'></div>臣之所深惧者，天下之权不在中书，必至溃裂四出，或在外戚，或在宦官，或在近习女宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1304387_comment'></div>唐之世进退大臣，听命阉寺，流弊之极，遂有定策国老者出焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1304387_comment'></div>臣言及此，不胜履霜坚冰之忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1304387_comment'></div>陛下听之，宜为曲突徙薪之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1304387_comment'></div>何况绍定小人之渠魁，有表表在人耳目者，朵颐羊鼎之日久，钻头鼠穴之巧深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1304387_comment'></div>曩者予祠有命，举朝之士重足而立，交口而争，众怒难犯，成命遄寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1304387_comment'></div>今者无故又予之祠，岂冥冥之中有为之地者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1304387_comment'></div>臣谓世道升降之机，君子小人进退之会，但卜之宰辅何如人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1304387_comment'></div>为庆历、元祐，今日也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1304387_comment'></div>为崇、观、宣、政，亦今日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1304387_comment'></div>然为庆历、元祐则难，为崇、观、宣、政则易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1304387_comment'></div>天其或者与之，宿疴顿苏，筋力犹健，蒲轮一出，岂不副苍生霖雨之思？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1304387_comment'></div>如其不然，彼老奸者牵引而至，则天下之事去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1304387_comment'></div>臣去秋轮对，妄生臆料，惟恐曾布、韩忠彦不相能，而小人京得以求之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1304387_comment'></div>赵鼎、张浚不相下，而小人桧得以继之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1304387_comment'></div>使此狂言不幸而中，如宗庙社稷何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1304387_comment'></div>臣愿陛下审于择相，参以人望，毋为左右毁誉所惑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1304387_comment'></div>谨于用权，要使常在中书，毋为旁蹊曲径所移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1304387_comment'></div>一相得人，庶明励翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1304387_comment'></div>求所以当天心而合人心者，必以伸故王之冤、正远相之罪为第一义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1304387_comment'></div>前者二相虽所用有先后，均为受远相之知，岂无是非之心，而动有牵制，不得以直遂其欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1304387_comment'></div>今已用如性之、鸣复，召而未至如与之与夫人望所属之诸老，皆非托身于冰山者，必能陈大义以广上心，必能主纲常以扶世教，迁西溪之陵而即之高烁，择诸王之贤而主其奉尝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1304387_comment'></div>若夫弥远之家，纵不忍籍之，独不可籍其仆妾乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1304387_comment'></div>弥远之爵虽不忍追褫之，独不可诎其谥号乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1304387_comment'></div>弥远之子纵未欲禁锢之，独不可勒之休致乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1304387_comment'></div>执政大臣以大公存心，以中正许国，出一号令，行一赏罚，于其命令始出之地，其直如矢而又端之，其清如水而又澄之，则诸阃禀神算于帷幄，必不至于跋扈飞扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1304387_comment'></div>戚里妇寺近习之徒，受威令于朝堂，必不至于诪张为幻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1304387_comment'></div>而又旁招俊乂，列于庶位，以备经幄之讲论，以充扈从之顾问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1304387_comment'></div>君心正而朝廷正，而百官万民正，于以迓续皇天之命，于以简在宁考在天之灵，转灾为祥，易祸为福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1304387_comment'></div>臣所谓为庆历、元祐难者，则易将至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1304387_comment'></div>臣尝面睹清光，冒进人君不可欺天，人臣不可欺君之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1304387_comment'></div>陛下温颜容纳，不斥不怒，畀以祠廪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1304387_comment'></div>甫及踰年，又起家以半刺宠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1304387_comment'></div>隆天厚地，恩德难酬，寸草报春，寤寐在念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1304387_comment'></div>窃见先朝名臣司马光通判并州日，当仁宗春秋方富，而首抗建储，大议乃定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1304387_comment'></div>其时在朝公卿所难言者，而光言之，仁宗不以位卑言高罪之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1304387_comment'></div>臣才品庸陋，于光无能为役，然葵藿向阳，心实同之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1304387_comment'></div>敢因明诏之下，控竭胸臆，冒进狂言，亦惟恃陛下有仁宗之明，故臣得以效光之直也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1304387_comment'></div>干犯天威，罪当万死，惟陛下赦之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_135_1304387_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6395b73bd2544692b7373d6e29a64514_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6395b73bd2544692b7373d6e29a64514");'><span id='6395b73bd2544692b7373d6e29a64514_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1219&endYear=1219')">1219年</a>，36岁</div><div id='6395b73bd2544692b7373d6e29a64514' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1219&endYear=1219')">1219年</a>　年底，过隆兴府，上启拜见见真德秀。作品：《见江西真帅启》<div id='poem_1304394' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304394' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304394?labeling=true' target='_blank'>见江西真帅启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1219年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304394")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304394_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304394'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304394'>平生漫刺，懒趋金、张、许、史之门墙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304394_comment'></div>远戍迁车，愿识杜、范、欧、韩之人物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304394_comment'></div>虽匪在受察受容之数，实久劳起敬起慕之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304394_comment'></div>谋三釜粟之未皇，持一瓣香之为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304394_comment'></div>窃以百年荣悴，同归于尽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304394_comment'></div>万世议论，有是与非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304394_comment'></div>想孔光、张禹之诸人，尚有馀臭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304394_comment'></div>读李膺、杜乔之诸传，至今耿光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304394_comment'></div>方当沦胥于流俗之中，而有特立于时贤之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304394_comment'></div>稍具识见，皆知依归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304394_comment'></div>恭惟某官大明若揭日月而行，细行亦通神明之奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304394_comment'></div>明体达用，传心程氏之诸书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304394_comment'></div>开诚布公，尚友孔明于千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304394_comment'></div>在闺门则怡颜养志，立朝廷则正色责难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304394_comment'></div>鲠论危言，兴起南渡积年之弱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304394_comment'></div>忠肝义胆，对越列圣在天之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304394_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1304394_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1304394'><span class='label'>按：</span>原本阙。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1304394_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
长沙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a486421f3a4b40f9a39df023342a1c27_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a486421f3a4b40f9a39df023342a1c27");'><span id='a486421f3a4b40f9a39df023342a1c27_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1220&endYear=1221')">1220-1221年</a>，37-38岁</div><div id='a486421f3a4b40f9a39df023342a1c27' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1220&endYear=1220')">1220年</a>　为潭州观察推官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1220&endYear=1220')">1220年</a>　上启拜见邹应龙。作品：《贺邹帅给事启》<div id='poem_1304396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304396?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺邹帅给事启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1220年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304396")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304396'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304396'>绿邸藉纶，红牙易阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304396_comment'></div>烦公护太子，久焉思羽翼之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304396_comment'></div>借君重淮阳，示以归禁闼之渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304396_comment'></div>湘灵起舞，岳后前驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304396_comment'></div>恭惟某官道传至圣大贤之心，文续先秦古书之脉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304396_comment'></div>虎榜首登，凤池身到，固地位之宜然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304396_comment'></div>鳌头宠重，鹤发恩深，尤人生之鲜俪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304396_comment'></div>付科名于馀事，守节义之大闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304396_comment'></div>方鼠穴权门，趋者成市，而螭坳直笔，屹然如山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304396_comment'></div>及调更化之弦，时方多事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304396_comment'></div>独卫出疆之璧，义不辞难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304396_comment'></div>入还班行，进掌封驳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304396_comment'></div>谁不批敕，鲜有如何郯之力争；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304396_comment'></div>因此结知，故每见邹浩而辄喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304396_comment'></div>居中未久，丐外即行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304396_comment'></div>国事日新，比贞观初年之何若；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304396_comment'></div>君子一去，觉贞元朝士之无多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304396_comment'></div>心变阙以常丹，发忧边而渐白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304396_comment'></div>惟有甘棠之蔽芾，远到海头；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304396_comment'></div>最宜丛桂之婆娑，久留春脚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304396_comment'></div>欢声无地可著，最课为天简和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304396_comment'></div>太史夜占，喜长沙之星见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304396_comment'></div>行人朝发，趣衡岳之云开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304396_comment'></div>宝阁升大学士之班，轻车奉太夫人之养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304396_comment'></div>众皆争先而称贺，仆知大用之有阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1304396_comment'></div>盖当夷夏消长之交，未决战和依违之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1304396_comment'></div>《春秋》复雠之义大，乃素学之欲行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1304396_comment'></div>英俊在朝则本强，正善类之所属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1304396_comment'></div>有以中书何无寇公为问者，当以吾国即相司马而答之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1304396_comment'></div>初立本奇，更好黄花之晚节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1304396_comment'></div>傥来不计，直垂汗竹之芳名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1304396_comment'></div>伏念某读书不多，合世更寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1304396_comment'></div>比奉槐枫之对，空臆尽言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1304396_comment'></div>不知草茅之疏，转喉触讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1304396_comment'></div>甘输三筹而不悔，仅忝一命以进身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1304396_comment'></div>冬已及于瓜期，夏方趋于莲幕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1304396_comment'></div>始仕曰筮，或者即初而觇终；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1304396_comment'></div>事长必忠，安敢以顺而为正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1304396_comment'></div>竦闻元帅，来镇此方，幸以邻壤之诸生，得为油幢之末吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1304396_comment'></div>虽素于左右，本无介绍，然见之方册，不昧平生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1304396_comment'></div>况进士题名，既接凤雏之武；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1304396_comment'></div>而小人有母，敢希燕喜之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1304396_comment'></div>傥推老吾老、幼吾幼之心，当无中不中、才不才之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1304396_comment'></div>曲怜臭味，俾托帡幪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1304396_comment'></div>待我不以众人，倘少垂于异眄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1304396_comment'></div>因主可以信客，窃自激于懦衷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1304396_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1221&endYear=1221')">1221年3月</a>　潭州善化县尉司新廨建成，为作记。作品：《潭州善化县尉司新廨记》<div id='poem_1304575' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304575' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304575?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潭州善化县尉司新廨记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1221年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304575")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304575_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304575'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304575'>官无小，苟以家事视官事者，皆可书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304575_comment'></div>善化特长沙一宽乡耳，绍圣中始析而为县，因乡以名之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304575_comment'></div>于是省长沙、湘潭二丞为之令，省长沙东尉为之簿，至于尉则独无所省于彼，而不得不为之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304575_comment'></div>夫以始立之邑、创置之官，则其力必不暇致美于一廨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304575_comment'></div>今庐陵汤君克诚秋视篆而冬惟筑，非以家事视官事者，其孰能之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304575_comment'></div>廨旧在定居门外，浮屠逼于旁，神祠殿于后，于阴阳勿协。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304575_comment'></div>且厥壤卑湿，屋老栋桡，居者为之不宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304575_comment'></div>君始至，僦屋以居，亟请于州，丐迁于阅圃中之隙地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304575_comment'></div>大帅文昌叶公可之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304575_comment'></div>建屋三十楹，糜金钱五十万，郡邑无丝粟助，编户无分毫扰，皆君出力为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304575_comment'></div>独有朴士唐世英者尝德于君，推吾侪犹有阖庐以辟寒暑之心，以木之堪为杗栋榱栌者四十株乐输之，以相其用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304575_comment'></div>廨之成实嘉定辛巳三月之朔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304575_comment'></div>凡廨葺旧非难，舍旧而图新为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304575_comment'></div>世之穷官显宦月俸盈车，尚间有视官宇如传舍，勿支勿补，谓无预吾事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304575_comment'></div>尉俸入几何，虽苦节犹不足于用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304575_comment'></div>又其职比他曹其事尤夥，警椎剽，捕窃攘，察讼系，长吏文檄无虚日，居官者惧不给命，不免于戾，而何堪此役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304575_comment'></div>今君费己以宁人，劳今以佚后，其心荦荦与流俗不同，于此可得其槩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304575_comment'></div>而世率谓官小者不足以行志，自君视之，其然岂其然乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304575_comment'></div>余于此抑重有感也，好善恶不善，天下人情本不相远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304575_comment'></div>苟一毫不安于心，不改为之不止，可欲之善最于此乎见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304575_comment'></div>今少公之廨，地则更淤洳而为刚燥矣，室则更偪隘而为高明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304575_comment'></div>汤君又能夙夜振职，凡政之不便于民者，悉禀于长而更新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304575_comment'></div>后来者观室则念君之恩勤，一日必葺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304575_comment'></div>观政则寻君之矩矱，一利害必究心，庶无负于君今日之所以遗后人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304575_comment'></div>不然，其室日新，其政日陋，玩愒书满，翩然而去，宁不愧见于壁门之记云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1304575_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1221&endYear=1221')">1221年</a>　纪念胡安国、张栻二先生祠堂建成，为作记。作品：《胡文定张宣公二先生祠堂记》<div id='poem_1304573' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304573' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304573?labeling=true' target='_blank'>胡文定张宣公二先生祠堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1221年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304573")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304573_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304573'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304573'>道德性命之学，自孟氏后，传者失其宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304573_comment'></div>国朝周夫子始唱于道之濂溪，程、张诸儒广其传为关洛学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304573_comment'></div>潭于道犹洙鲁而近，独未有疏导濂溪一派以泽湘人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304573_comment'></div>崇宁间，胡文定以提湖南学事道出湘乡，迁县学于东南隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304573_comment'></div>淳熙间张宣公帅桂林，迂道访文定旧迹，进诸生而教之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304573_comment'></div>于是师友渊源，泓涵演迤，得视关洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304573_comment'></div>嘉定己卯，邑宰林侯得中实来，知所先务，顾瞻芹藻为旧甘棠，慨然叹曰：「《礼》言祭有道德者于瞽宗，谓国学也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304573_comment'></div>《传》言祭乡先生于社，谓乡学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304573_comment'></div>惟二先生既蒙谥于朝，瞽宗祠典必以次举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304573_comment'></div>而是邑典刑模范，近接耳目，若不以义起礼，立祠学宫，是忘二先生所以私淑者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304573_comment'></div>方与学职共筹之，会邑士萧君佐以其事白于计使赵公汝谠，公忻然出帑金捐材木，怂恿其决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304573_comment'></div>庚辰秋，祠堂成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304573_comment'></div>明年林侯贻书，嘱某为识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304573_comment'></div>某窃惟文定之于伊川先生，盖闻而知之者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304573_comment'></div>宣公之于五峰先生，盖见而知之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304573_comment'></div>其学以忠孝为本，而敬以行之，笔之于书，授之于徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304573_comment'></div>语小辨析义利，毫釐必谨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304573_comment'></div>语大功用宏阔，人纪赖以扶植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304573_comment'></div>当其时，不惟学士大夫得所矜式，而闾巷小民亦相戒不为不义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304573_comment'></div>至今经行之地，遗迹未陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304573_comment'></div>诗书之泽渊乎涟水，不足言其深也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304573_comment'></div>教学之功崒乎凤山，不足言其高也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304573_comment'></div>且自崇、观以来，公卿达官追趋逐嗜，不知其几，至今人犹羞称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304573_comment'></div>惟文定公在仕版四十年，实历不盈六考；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304573_comment'></div>宣公蚤被阜陵知遇，骎骎大用，竟以排权贵去国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1304573_comment'></div>一时禄秩，视德弗称，百世之下，清风凛然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1304573_comment'></div>士之藏修息游于斯者，盍知所择矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1304573_comment'></div>侯三山人，擢壬戌进士第，雅志好修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1304573_comment'></div>学之大成殿与从祀两庑，悉更新之，外植门观，尤壮伟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1304573_comment'></div>是祠之建，其《诗》所谓「高山仰止，景行行止」者欤？</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1304573_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1221&endYear=1221')">1221年</a>　在潭州任上，上启拜见湖南叶帅。作品：《通湖南叶帅启》<div id='poem_1304395' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304395' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304395?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通湖南叶帅启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1221年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304395")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304395_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304395'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304395'>辍文昌之座以帅藩，稍缓召归之命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304395_comment'></div>着从事之衫而入幕，得为末席之宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304395_comment'></div>以明公一日之去留，卜贱子终身之遇否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304395_comment'></div>仕莫重乎始进，天固使之有依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304395_comment'></div>恭惟某官气大而养以刚，道高而立于独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304395_comment'></div>渠渠孝行，每兴感于《蓼莪》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304395_comment'></div>皦皦科名，曾收功于药笼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304395_comment'></div>守命义之大节，为出处之宏图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304395_comment'></div>凫舄横飞，鸳行增重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304395_comment'></div>考容台三千礼，司蕝甚闲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304395_comment'></div>为册府第一官，采芸有味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304395_comment'></div>方在开禧嘉定之际，是为君子小人之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304395_comment'></div>一贤峨豸以当前，众正得舆而交贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304395_comment'></div>直声大振，雷轰电击于奸未去之先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304395_comment'></div>元气不伤，风恬雨霁于事已定之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304395_comment'></div>䌷秘史于金匮石室，导正学于广厦细旃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304395_comment'></div>履声上迫于云霄，斧绣下临于阈阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304395_comment'></div>利源竭矣，谁能宽之一分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304395_comment'></div>仁人耻之，不待去于三宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304395_comment'></div>此举盈庭之色动，未几前席之恩深，爰屈台斗之光，俯照沙星之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304395_comment'></div>潭府甚淳古，分少陵岳麓之清；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304395_comment'></div>客堂喜空凉，和吏部湘川之句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304395_comment'></div>政成而棠阴密，讼简而銗筒稀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304395_comment'></div>然当远郊营垒之相望，岂容明堂梁栋之小用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304395_comment'></div>右诸道之奏最，隐若长城；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1304395_comment'></div>左一席之久虚，行膺显册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1304395_comment'></div>伏念某晚未见道，穷坐为儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1304395_comment'></div>百战蚁酣，敢望锥囊之先露；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1304395_comment'></div>一朝胪唱，滥叨铛脚之后尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1304395_comment'></div>父毡尚青而复还，母发已白而待养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1304395_comment'></div>若以苟禄仕则仅可，漫不知幕辩者为何幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1304395_comment'></div>以部封下之旧民，而为油幢底之新吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1304395_comment'></div>始仕曰筮，或者即初而觇终；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1304395_comment'></div>事长必忠，焉敢以顺而为正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1304395_comment'></div>惟矜其臭味之似，而许以帡幪之归，庶逭官箴，可谐亲养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1304395_comment'></div>乌公鈇钺之下，倘见礼于温生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1304395_comment'></div>和相衣钵之传，窃有心于范质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1304395_comment'></div>渎尊冒昧，拊己凌兢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1304395_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1221&endYear=1221')">1221年</a>　在潭州任上，上启拜见湘潭监酒右弁。作品：《与湘潭监酒右弁启》<div id='poem_1304405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与湘潭监酒右弁启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1221年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304405")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304405_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304405'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304405'>为米五斗而漫来，何裨婉画；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304405_comment'></div>有酝三升之可恋，获缀英游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304405_comment'></div>贺上滞迟，先施倒置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304405_comment'></div>恭惟某官沉酣方虎之略，糟粕孙吴之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304405_comment'></div>暂韬厥光，来隐于酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304405_comment'></div>虽养高此地，不妨吊灵均英魄之独醒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304405_comment'></div>然右武之时，谁肯持将军告身而易醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304405_comment'></div>小而投醪士卒，大则作醴庙堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304405_comment'></div>行且见之，非为佞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304405_comment'></div>某寒酸可笑，艰苦备尝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304405_comment'></div>来傍莲池，陋矣斗筲之器；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304405_comment'></div>粗营菽水，苟焉钟釜之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304405_comment'></div>幸甚同僚之得贤，先拜高文之有味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304405_comment'></div>自此作乞浆之请，愿一中之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304405_comment'></div>何时定饮酎之交，永为好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304405_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1304405_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1221&endYear=1221')">1221年</a>　在潭州任上，上启拜见醴陵刘宰。作品：《与醴陵刘宰启》<div id='poem_1304406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与醴陵刘宰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1221年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304406")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304406'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304406'>行役三千里，来依幕府之芙蓉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304406_comment'></div>入境第一程，首访河阳之桃李。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304406_comment'></div>先睹为快，以名自通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304406_comment'></div>恭惟某官籍甚月评，穹其天分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304406_comment'></div>《七略》总百家之绪，世美可寻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304406_comment'></div>千年六一翁之乡，风流未泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304406_comment'></div>裹以冠裳而不任，直于翰墨以策勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304406_comment'></div>神人换鼻而许以正郎，朱吏点头而畀以上第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304406_comment'></div>荐游邛莋，慨然忘蜀道之难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304406_comment'></div>继董布泉，去又作雪山之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304406_comment'></div>合即坐三馆之上矣，乃廉取百里而宰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304406_comment'></div>今士夫厌汤镬之焦熬，相顾瑟缩，明执事施硎刀于肯綮，了无留难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304406_comment'></div>寓抚字之意于琴中，息嚚讼之风于棠下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304406_comment'></div>盖大冯君宜春之遗爱，今犹思之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304406_comment'></div>而鲁仲康中牟之政声，雅亦称是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304406_comment'></div>一同幸甚，三异蔼然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304406_comment'></div>行膺黄纸之除书，更与青毡而出色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304406_comment'></div>有如某者，见谓斐然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304406_comment'></div>文场曾被于百疮，仅收末效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304406_comment'></div>宦海方航于一苇，未识前津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304406_comment'></div>幸假道于名区，有指踪之素宦，愿出绪馀以告，用为画诺之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304406_comment'></div>岂无同僚之尽心，不若先入者为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304406_comment'></div>仕大国而交英俊，快平昔之襟期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304406_comment'></div>在武城而闻弦歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304406_comment'></div>动书生之技痒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1304406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1221&endYear=1221')">1221年</a>　在潭州任上，上启拜见湘阴李宰。作品：《与湘阴李宰启》<div id='poem_1304407' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304407' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304407?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与湘阴李宰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1221年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304407")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304407_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304407'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304407'>子来几日，方依幕府之芙蓉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304407_comment'></div>彼美一人，剩种河阳之桃李。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304407_comment'></div>未敕墨卿之敬，乃为签府所先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304407_comment'></div>恭惟某官阀冠云霄，胸罗星宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304407_comment'></div>家岂不置《文选》，耻争寒士之科名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304407_comment'></div>世皆称有天才，宛似谪仙之风骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304407_comment'></div>自初膴仕，总是名藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304407_comment'></div>勾稽馀闲，诗思蜚扬于滕阁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304407_comment'></div>平反一笑，阴功㳽渺于吴江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304407_comment'></div>凭铁瓮以饷师，向金闺而彻籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304407_comment'></div>便合在六察之上矣，乃廉取百里而宰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304407_comment'></div>今士夫厌汤镬之焦熬，相顾瑟缩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304407_comment'></div>明执事施硎刀之肯綮，了无留难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304407_comment'></div>锦愈濯而愈鲜，琴一弹而一韵，政异遂雉雏之乐，官清任马骨之高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304407_comment'></div>政声满湘之南，作诸邑样；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304407_comment'></div>名节自天而下，登要路津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304407_comment'></div>某读书不多，合世更寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304407_comment'></div>元龙空有湖海之气，司马倦作山川之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304407_comment'></div>仰破屋以哦诗，呕肝不悔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304407_comment'></div>俯大廷而对策，空臆尽言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304407_comment'></div>儒科仅窃于还丹，世味殆如于嚼蜡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304407_comment'></div>冬已告戍，夏方抵官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304407_comment'></div>胡迟其行，盖恐面墙于涖事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304407_comment'></div>或赞吾决，谓有大邑以庇身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304407_comment'></div>倘能矜臭味之同，必不吝箴规之诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1304407_comment'></div>公馀交贽，已窥君之一斑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1304407_comment'></div>何日盍簪，并授我以三昧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1304407_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1221&endYear=1221')">1221年</a>　在潭州任上，上启拜见湘乡林宰。作品：《与湘乡林宰启》<div id='poem_1304408' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304408' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304408?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与湘乡林宰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1221年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304408")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304408_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304408'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304408'>君乘车我戴笠，忆辇毂之相逢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304408_comment'></div>客遗鱼中有书，喜湖湘之共仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304408_comment'></div>入莲幕方数日许，望华封隔一水间，修敬辜迟，先施倒置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304408_comment'></div>恭惟某官望高胄子，学到儒先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304408_comment'></div>崔嵬双阙之家声，不断书种；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304408_comment'></div>呼吸三山之秀气，发为文词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304408_comment'></div>固尝于科目以策勋，乃耻与孤寒而争进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304408_comment'></div>取名廉甚，不妨兰菊之芬芳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304408_comment'></div>公论归之，合看蓬莱之步武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304408_comment'></div>乃飞双舄，来宰一同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304408_comment'></div>今士夫厌汤镬之焦熬，相顾瑟缩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304408_comment'></div>明执事施硎刀于肯綮，了无留难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304408_comment'></div>锦愈濯而愈鲜，琴一弹而一韵，政异遂雉雏之乐，官清任马骨之高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304408_comment'></div>期年报政之优，作诸邑样；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304408_comment'></div>一札自天而下，据要路津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304408_comment'></div>伏念某读书不多，合世更寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304408_comment'></div>大廷对策，妄陈忧国之孤忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304408_comment'></div>末第书名，何惜避人之三舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304408_comment'></div>冬月戍瓜之已及，夏初行李之方安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304408_comment'></div>胡迟其行，盖恐面墙于涖事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304408_comment'></div>或赞吾决，谓有大邑以庇身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304408_comment'></div>倘矜臭味之同，尚记游从之旧，必有忠告，俾逭官箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304408_comment'></div>想弦歌之声，忽动书生之技痒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304408_comment'></div>俟驺哄之至，拱聆官谱之绪馀。</div><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304409_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304409'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304409'>居桑梓乡，相去一牛鸣之地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304409_comment'></div>入芙蓉幕，孰知双凫舄之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304409_comment'></div>告至辜迟，先施倒置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304409_comment'></div>恭惟某官识高胄子，学到儒宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304409_comment'></div>笔搦虹霓，呼吸鼎山之秀气；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304409_comment'></div>名悬日月，峥嵘璧水之上游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304409_comment'></div>漫以毫芒，见之施设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304409_comment'></div>云深紫逻，大所居一尉之官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304409_comment'></div>草鞠圜扉，少亦活千人之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304409_comment'></div>蝉蜕七阶之选调，鹏骞万里之脩程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304409_comment'></div>今士夫厌汤镬之焦熬，相顾瑟缩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304409_comment'></div>驩声无地可着，溢为荐祢之章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304409_comment'></div>最课自天简知，行有徵黄之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304409_comment'></div>有如某者，见谓斐然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304409_comment'></div>仰破屋以哦诗，呕肝不悔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304409_comment'></div>俯大廷而对策，空臆尽言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304409_comment'></div>收科输鼎甲之三筹，初仕乏锥囊之一颖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304409_comment'></div>面墙必矣，指踪谁欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304409_comment'></div>惟大邑可以庇身，而乡人喜于见似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304409_comment'></div>愿出忠告，俾逭官箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304409_comment'></div>想弦歌之声，忽动书生之技痒；<div class='inline'
