class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304410'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304410'>湖南多宾客，漫来着从事之衫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304410_comment'></div>汝阳真天人，何尚墨男邦之绶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304410_comment'></div>未辨赫蹄而展庆，遽蒙绿绮之贻音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304410_comment'></div>恭惟某官派接天清，名垂斗灿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304410_comment'></div>去河间东平千载，得其盛心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304410_comment'></div>追太白长吉诸人，与之并驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304410_comment'></div>游戏文章之三昧，呈露政事之一班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304410_comment'></div>鸂鶒滩头，早协奇章之瑞谶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304410_comment'></div>松槐丛里，优为斯立之清游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304410_comment'></div>诸公挽之亨衢，荐墨纷乎盈箧，便合在六察之上矣，乃廉取百里而宰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304410_comment'></div>今士夫厌汤镬之焦熬，相顾瑟缩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304410_comment'></div>明执事施硎刀于肯綮，了无留难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304410_comment'></div>簸扬而糠在前，更张而琴有韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304410_comment'></div>官清如水，不妨马骨之高；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304410_comment'></div>最彻于天，好布鹓行之武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304410_comment'></div>有如某者，见谓斐然，弱惟殖学以代耕，贫止卖文而为活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304410_comment'></div>忤时对策，分输黄甲之三筹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304410_comment'></div>窃禄养亲，无补碧油之一画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304410_comment'></div>所赖臭味之无间，当有教诏以相规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304410_comment'></div>见君子心则夷，预知免矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304410_comment'></div>况大邑身所庇，窃有望焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1304410_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1221&endYear=1221')">1221年</a>　在潭州任上，上启拜见益阳尤宰。作品：《与益阳尤宰启》<div id='poem_1304411' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304411' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304411?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与益阳尤宰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1221年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304411")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304411_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304411'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304411'>佩服家声，愿识梁溪先生之裔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304411_comment'></div>讲闻县谱，熟知连城茂宰之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304411_comment'></div>彼此因王事之尘劳，往来略世俗之苛礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304411_comment'></div>将谓相诏以肝胆，胡为未忘于形骸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304411_comment'></div>一笺先施，百拜后诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304411_comment'></div>恭惟某官秀无可拣，敏莫能追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304411_comment'></div>宦学典刑，世有甘棠之笏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304411_comment'></div>风流蕴藉，人如濯柳之标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304411_comment'></div>篝灯诵有味书，下笔作惊人语，历仕皆膴，驰声甚休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304411_comment'></div>诸公挽之亨逵，荐剡纷乎盈箧，便合登六察之上矣，乃廉取百里而宰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304411_comment'></div>今士夫厌汤镬之焦熬，相顾瑟缩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304411_comment'></div>明执事施硎刀于肯綮，了无留难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304411_comment'></div>讼息而缿筒稀，政成而棠阴密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304411_comment'></div>官清如水，不妨马骨之高；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304411_comment'></div>秩满朝天，好布鹓行之武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304411_comment'></div>有如某者，见谓斐然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304411_comment'></div>仰破屋以哦诗，呕肝不悔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304411_comment'></div>俯大廷而对策，空臆尽言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304411_comment'></div>来傍莲池，苟营菽水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304411_comment'></div>惟是平生方介之癖，不学时样妩媚之妆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304411_comment'></div>幸大邑可以庇身，而素官宜于问政，必有忠告，俾逭官箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304411_comment'></div>想像弦歌，颇觉痒书生之技；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304411_comment'></div>闯闻驺哄，愿降见君子之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1304411_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1221&endYear=1221')">1221年</a>　在潭州任上，上启拜见长沙陈宰。作品：《与长沙陈宰启》<div id='poem_1304412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与长沙陈宰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1221年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304412")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304412_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304412'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304412'>入幕依芙蓉，方陪州从事之后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304412_comment'></div>满县栽桃李，喜聆乡先达之来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304412_comment'></div>昔愿见而未能，今相值则甚巧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304412_comment'></div>敬凭尺鲤，往白双凫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304412_comment'></div>恭惟某官天分穹然，月评籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304412_comment'></div>呼吸三山之秀气，发为雄文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304412_comment'></div>婆娑百尺之高楼，俯视馀子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304412_comment'></div>取科名如囊中物，试政事有肘后方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304412_comment'></div>䌽笔平反，少亦活千人之命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304412_comment'></div>剡章吹送，多其吐三语之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304412_comment'></div>趣觐清光，径升华秩，便合坐三雍之上矣，乃廉取百里而宰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304412_comment'></div>今士夫厌汤镬之焦熬，相顾瑟缩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304412_comment'></div>明执事施硎刀于肯綮，了无留难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304412_comment'></div>行将寓抚字之意于琴中，息嚚讼之风于棠下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304412_comment'></div>府邑甚淳古，必有三异之可书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304412_comment'></div>朝廷半老成，非久一同之借重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304412_comment'></div>有如某者，见谓斐然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304412_comment'></div>少尝慷慨于事功，壮则间关于场屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304412_comment'></div>大廷对策，妄陈忧国之孤忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304412_comment'></div>末第书名，何惜避人之三舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304412_comment'></div>来谋亲养，已过戍期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304412_comment'></div>胡迟其行，正恐素宦之无谱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304412_comment'></div>若有所恃，必得大邑以庇身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304412_comment'></div>倘忘年许以缔交，则暇日必有忠告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304412_comment'></div>一画一诺，仆焉方俯仰于人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1304412_comment'></div>有社有民，公也当施行所学。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1304412_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1221&endYear=1221')">1221年</a>　在潭州任上，上启拜见攸县权宰、周簿。作品：《与攸县权宰周簿启》<div id='poem_1304413' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304413' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304413?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与攸县权宰周簿启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1221年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304413")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304413_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304413'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304413'>依芙蓉而泛水，方陪诸从事之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304413_comment'></div>去枳棘而栽花，知有贵公子之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304413_comment'></div>辜迟告至，颠倒先施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304413_comment'></div>恭惟某官敏手莫追，清标特立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304413_comment'></div>传濂溪之学，源流河汉之深长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304413_comment'></div>生清献之乡，气类霜钟之感召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304413_comment'></div>方露厥颖于政事，已雷其声于搢绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304413_comment'></div>人之为言，以立身矮屋而称屈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304413_comment'></div>事当其会，有不善制锦而见伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304413_comment'></div>方当路弄印而熟筹，谓执事改弦而可理，果能支欹补罅，顿使易听改观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304413_comment'></div>簸扬而糠在前，盘错而器愈利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304413_comment'></div>县自有谱，想得诸家法者甚详；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304413_comment'></div>时正需材，当寘彼周行而后快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304413_comment'></div>有如某者，见谓斐然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304413_comment'></div>仰破屋以哦诗，呕肝不悔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304413_comment'></div>俯大廷而对策，空臆尽言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304413_comment'></div>分输黄甲之三筹，无补碧油之一画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304413_comment'></div>面墙必矣，指踪茫然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304413_comment'></div>幸已缔好于棣华，独未一瞻于芝宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304413_comment'></div>闯闻驺哄，愿降见君子之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304413_comment'></div>想像弦歌，颇觉痒书生之技。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1304413_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1221&endYear=1221')">1221年</a>　在潭州任上，有启文回湘乡黄七举县尉。作品：《回湘乡黄尉（七举）启》<div id='poem_1304414' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304414' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304414?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回湘乡黄尉<span class='inlineComment2'>（七举）</span>启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1221年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304414")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304414_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304414'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304414'>辇毂相逢，犹记洒慈恩之墨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304414_comment'></div>湖湘始仕，同来着从事之衫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304414_comment'></div>以幕府文书之方殷，为少公翰墨所先辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304414_comment'></div>倒置太甚，不敏何言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304414_comment'></div>恭惟某官天分穹窿，学力宏毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304414_comment'></div>使国人有所式，太学称为官样之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304414_comment'></div>思天下犹己饥，微时已试活人之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304414_comment'></div>科举惟垂于蜗饵，场屋如掷于雉卢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304414_comment'></div>妄男子侥倖成名，一战而霸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304414_comment'></div>真将军偃蹇不偶，七纵乃擒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304414_comment'></div>方以格拘，暂焉仙隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304414_comment'></div>五色棒定优于巡檄，一县花必预于栽培。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304414_comment'></div>鸂鶒双飞，好报金滩之瑞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304414_comment'></div>孔鸾齐列，行通玉陛之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304414_comment'></div>某读书不多，合世更寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304414_comment'></div>向尝吐危言而对策，以讦见排；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304414_comment'></div>今复持直道以事人，似狂未醒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304414_comment'></div>所喜联事，而有同盟，必不金玉其音，时出药石之诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304414_comment'></div>州县徒劳耳，俱未免俯仰于人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304414_comment'></div>富贵何有哉，要相期远大之业<span class='inlineComment2'>（《臞轩集》卷六。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304414_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1304414'>题下原有注云：「黄未第时招米舟济饥，得赏，既第，用此关升从事郎」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1304414_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
晋江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f06d0022a49543ec95ffd36bc1d17c22_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f06d0022a49543ec95ffd36bc1d17c22");'><span id='f06d0022a49543ec95ffd36bc1d17c22_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1232&endYear=1233')">1232-1233年</a>，49-50岁</div><div id='f06d0022a49543ec95ffd36bc1d17c22' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1232&endYear=1232')">1232年</a>　任南外睦宗院教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1233&endYear=1233')">1233年</a>　真德秀荐举赴都堂审察，上启致谢。作品：《谢真师荐举启》<div id='poem_1304463' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304463' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304463?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢真师荐举启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1233年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304463")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304463_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304463'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304463'>开藩旬日，方罗幕府之群英；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304463_comment'></div>荐剡一封，首及墙屏之下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304463_comment'></div>识者以为公举，众人则曰私恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304463_comment'></div>退自省循，独有感慨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304463_comment'></div>惟师生以道而合，与宾主之分不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304463_comment'></div>彦明授业于伊川，本无干禄之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304463_comment'></div>器之执经于涑水，非为荐求之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304463_comment'></div>天爵重则人爵可轻，义荣贵则势荣可贱，有宁终其身之弗遇，不忍叛所学以苟容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304463_comment'></div>如某之愚，从公也久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304463_comment'></div>孺子可教，初拜南昌之赠言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304463_comment'></div>门人益亲，屡造西山而问道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304463_comment'></div>所谓晦斯明窒斯通之席，喜得于学不厌诲不倦之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304463_comment'></div>昔年盛而气盈，今霜降而水涸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304463_comment'></div>来倚麟庠之席，获依燕寝之香，瞬养息存，日省月试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304463_comment'></div>穷理致用之训，朝以书绅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304463_comment'></div>习静持敬之方，夕而铭几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304463_comment'></div>苟有立命安身之地，敢为贪荣希进之图！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304463_comment'></div>及牙纛之莅三神山，叹蓬莱之隔一弱水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304463_comment'></div>忽闻邮置，特赐衮褒，岂察其学业之渐成，亦望其德业之少试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304463_comment'></div>盖知仲淹之贤则必荐，遑及其他；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304463_comment'></div>而为安定之学者非迂，觊施诸用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304463_comment'></div>此相期之盛意，不敢望于他人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304463_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官诚立而明通，操约而施普。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304463_comment'></div>鸿辞丽藻，续麟笔之正传；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304463_comment'></div>宝匣瑶琴，嗣龙门之遗响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1304463_comment'></div>忧国之心愈渴，阅士之眼弥高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1304463_comment'></div>方将以此身任当世之经纶，亦必勉其徒以大人之事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1304463_comment'></div>高文行远而谓某有甚蔚之词章，直气蟠空而谓某有不阿之议论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1304463_comment'></div>何以当此，窃有请焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1304463_comment'></div>今天下之所少非文，士君子之最难者节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1304463_comment'></div>居上位者既喜佞而恶戆，在下寮者多毁方而为圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1304463_comment'></div>郑公良臣，不乐义方有太直之行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1304463_comment'></div>曲江英宰，且嫌挺之负苦劲之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1304463_comment'></div>所愿先生秉钧轴之权，博取吾党有气节之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1304463_comment'></div>某益思植立，愈励操修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1304463_comment'></div>表里同源，敢不推立言之诚而立德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1304463_comment'></div>阿谀深耻，又当移事师之忠以事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1304463_comment'></div>惟能为人，是报知己。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1304463_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
漳州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='aec491b5afa84138b1a6fba343e6430a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aec491b5afa84138b1a6fba343e6430a");'><span id='aec491b5afa84138b1a6fba343e6430a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1237')">1236-1237年</a>，53-54岁</div><div id='aec491b5afa84138b1a6fba343e6430a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年冬</a>　改秩通判漳州。作品：《漳倅到任告先圣文》<div id='poem_1304631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>漳倅到任告先圣文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1236年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304631")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304631_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304631'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304631'>某学古而迂，身谋甚左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304631_comment'></div>一第廿年，方书六考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304631_comment'></div>贵岂不欲，耻非其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304631_comment'></div>富不可求，从吾所好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304631_comment'></div>圣谟洋洋，惟知允蹈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304631_comment'></div>拜庙之辰，敢以必告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304631_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1304631'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1304631_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年10月</a>　在漳州生日有诗。作品：《生朝止客》<div id='poem_71034' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71034' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71034?labeling=true' target='_blank'>生朝止客</a><span class='authorDate'>（1236年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_71034")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_71034_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_71034'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71034'>白发苍颜五十三，北风不竞又来南。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71034'>宦情于我蜡来淡，世味从渠蜜样甘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71034'>乌哺劬劳恩未报，雁行凄断痛何堪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71034'>记生纵有一樽酒，忍与妻孥共醉酣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71034'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_71034_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年12月</a>　腊月，有《清漳文会录序》<div id='poem_1304546' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304546' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304546?labeling=true' target='_blank'>清漳文会录序</a><span class='authorDate'>（端平三年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304546")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304546_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304546'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304546'>礼有来学而无往教，教而至于往，道之轻甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304546_comment'></div>拾经生之陈言，缀史氏之腐说，闻者望望而去，则其取轻也固宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304546_comment'></div>今吾友德载之讲本朝典故也，䌷绎乎瑶编宝帙之文，采摭乎稗官野史之纪，参之以元夫钜人崇论闳议，而以己见断之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304546_comment'></div>所至皋比一设，朋簪翕随，所谓不即人而人自即之者，孰得以议吾道之轻哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304546_comment'></div>漳为诸老讲学之地，风教所渐，杰乂辈出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304546_comment'></div>德载毋谓邾小而易之，解颐之誉、折角之嘲，二者必有一于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304546_comment'></div>丙申腊月序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1304546_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年3月</a>　三月，魏了翁卒，作文祭之。作品：《祭魏鹤山先生文》<div id='poem_1304622' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304622' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304622?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭魏鹤山先生文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304622")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304622_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304622'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304622'>惟国家盛时之人才，禀山川清淑之间气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304622_comment'></div>文章则眉山之父子，道学则伊川之昆季。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304622_comment'></div>更南渡之百年，邈徽称而谁嗣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304622_comment'></div>鹤山先生以英伟之姿，抱远大之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304622_comment'></div>文追正始之音，学探圣贤之秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304622_comment'></div>权史当朝，以儒为戏，先生辈人，不得行志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304622_comment'></div>当宝庆之初元，抗纲常之宏议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304622_comment'></div>虎守关而怒号，犬见日而群吠，斥忠质于渠阳，快女媭之怨詈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304622_comment'></div>谊也当此，赋鵩以悲鸣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304622_comment'></div>原也当此，沉湘而憔悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304622_comment'></div>先生处之泰然，曰吾有命有义，履畏境如康庄，茹苦荼如甘荠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304622_comment'></div>独尽力于斯文，将垂光于来世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304622_comment'></div>于《易》则探赜钩深，于《礼》则订讹證伪，于诗则陶写襟灵，于字则平章篆隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304622_comment'></div>凡笔端之游嬉，指理窟而超诣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304622_comment'></div>积八年之深功，续程苏之位置，使一朝之大用，当尽抒于经济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304622_comment'></div>迨夫天毙权奸，朝登儒揆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304622_comment'></div>初年而西山自闽来，次年而先生自蜀至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304622_comment'></div>洪、蒋诸贤，后先征汇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304622_comment'></div>遂使端平之初，及见元祐之懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304622_comment'></div>奈西山之一颓，如杲日之西坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304622_comment'></div>先生哭之尽哀，人士闻之兴喟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304622_comment'></div>未几而蒋终于家，又未几而洪薨于位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304622_comment'></div>立东门者一人，凛灵光之标致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304622_comment'></div>以政地之重臣，为督府之元帅，何异乎嫉真卿而使之为说李之行，恶彦国而使之为出疆之使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304622_comment'></div>未视师而贼胆寒，将策勋而同列忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1304622_comment'></div>俄异论之横生，怅初心之莫遂，蜀无家之可归，奉丛祠之若寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1304622_comment'></div>及帅闽之命颁，犹物情之少慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1304622_comment'></div>司封驳者何人，犯清议而不愧！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1304622_comment'></div>使此身之犹存，尚行道之可冀，何殒星之告妖，乃翛然而蝉蜕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1304622_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1304622_comment'></div>天生伟人，关系匪细，出处则关民生之戚休，存亡则系吾道之兴废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1304622_comment'></div>宜锡之期颐之年，留以为宗社之卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1304622_comment'></div>至于奸臣弄权，贪夫败类，宜凶于而身而家，毋得以为鬼为魅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1304622_comment'></div>彼苍者天，胡然不惠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1304622_comment'></div>恶者永年，善者降厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1304622_comment'></div>望之、周堪殁，而孔光赐杖于建平之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1304622_comment'></div>元城、莹中卒，而蔡京白首于靖康之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1304622_comment'></div>钟鸣漏尽者冥行不休，而元夫巨人乃沦亡而相继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1304622_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1304622_comment'></div>国步间关，民生彫弊，京襄邱墟，江淮鼎沸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1304622_comment'></div>外有侧目伺隙之憸壬，内有摇舌肆谗之妇寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1304622_comment'></div>此何时而梁木摧，此何景而蛟龙逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1304622_comment'></div>是殆晋人所谓秋高摇落之时，使人眩然而出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1304622_comment'></div>某晚登门墙，辱窥小异，虽名位之不侔，偶襟期之胥契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1304622_comment'></div>读奏篇之瞽言，曰差强乎人意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1304622_comment'></div>属霜简之见排，纷群目之疾视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1304622_comment'></div>先生白之榻前，至色庄而言毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1304622_comment'></div>谓去一微臣不足怜，恐天下自此以为讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1304622_comment'></div>旋开悟于上心，得免投之荒裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1304622_comment'></div>赠之以朝阳鸣凤之绣图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1304622_comment'></div>申之以彩笔飞鸾之大字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1304622_comment'></div>至今序引之珍藏，烨然有光于巾笥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1304622_comment'></div>先生于仆非纳交，仆于先生非借势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1304622_comment'></div>或者下石之未休，犹谓托名流而附丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1304622_comment'></div>自漳滨而斥还，拟墓前而自誓，抱直道以不渝，鞭古心而愈励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1304622_comment'></div>闻讣告于邮传，集百忧于肝肺，盖为世道之隐忧，非特一身之私计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1304622_comment'></div>假精庐以招魂，陈生刍而设祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1304622_comment'></div>谅英爽之周游，如源泉之在地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1304622_comment'></div>随感召而必通，傥下歆乎一酹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1304622_comment'></div>人之云亡，邦国殄瘁，悠悠我思，明发不寐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_59_1304622_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　有词迎接友人方大琮。作品：《沁园春（迎方右史德润）》<div id='poem_71364' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71364' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71364?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沁园春 迎方右史德润</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_71364")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_71364_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_71364'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71364'>首尾四年，台省好官，都做一回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71364'>便前头更有，合当做底，何妨且恁，猛省归来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71364'>甲第新成，开尊行乐，脆管繁弦十二钗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71364'>回头笑，这狂生无用，削尽官阶。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71364_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71364'>狂生真个狂哉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_71364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_71364'>泼性气年来全未灰。<div id='poem_sentence_5_71364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_71364'>有龙鳞凤翼，不能攀附，牛衣渔具，早已安排。<div id='poem_sentence_6_71364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_71364'>烂煮园蔬，熟煨山芋，白发苍颜穷秀才。<div id='poem_sentence_7_71364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_71364'>官休做，莫狂无处著，送去琼崖。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_71364_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　友人郑寅卒，作文祭之。作品：《祭郑都承子敬文（丁酉）》<div id='poem_1304624' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304624' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304624?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭郑都承子敬文<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　丁酉）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304624")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304624_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304624'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304624'>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304624_comment'></div>仲春初浣，方得公书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304624_comment'></div>情文溢纸，细字渠渠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304624_comment'></div>谓因感冷，药裹是需。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304624_comment'></div>我每羡公，精于调理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304624_comment'></div>红颜怡怡，高谈亹亹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304624_comment'></div>纵有微疴，亦偶然尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304624_comment'></div>一日行路，忽有异传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304624_comment'></div>我不敢信，心极悬悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304624_comment'></div>徐诘其寔，公果溘然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304624_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304624_comment'></div>公生相门，寔则儒素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304624_comment'></div>涵茹群书，练习典故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304624_comment'></div>不但多闻，且通世务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304624_comment'></div>太和试邑，蔼有休称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304624_comment'></div>入迁院辖，再转为丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304624_comment'></div>显宦要职，跬步可登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304624_comment'></div>维时权奸，其门可炙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304624_comment'></div>公心耻之，抗章丐出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304624_comment'></div>吾官宁卑，吾道不屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304624_comment'></div>高牙大纛，作牧庐陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304624_comment'></div>民肌春暖，吏胆冰凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304624_comment'></div>不畏强御，谗言朋兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304624_comment'></div>浩然来归，一邱一壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304624_comment'></div>与陈复斋，追随最乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1304624_comment'></div>罔俾耆英，专美于洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1304624_comment'></div>十有七载，冰山乃倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1304624_comment'></div>遄以郎召，承旨枢庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1304624_comment'></div>一语不合，拂袖而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1304624_comment'></div>有诏起家，畀以漳守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1304624_comment'></div>政痁民疵，是图是究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1304624_comment'></div>千里咏歌，二天宏覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1304624_comment'></div>乃者望日，出劝农耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1304624_comment'></div>归坐铃阁，寝已三更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1304624_comment'></div>曾谓顷刻，乃隔死生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1304624_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1304624_comment'></div>贤者存亡，有关天运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1304624_comment'></div>比年以来，德星屡殒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1304624_comment'></div>我欲问天，天不可问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1304624_comment'></div>复斋冢木，郁乎苍烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1304624_comment'></div>建昌仙去，闾里凄然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1304624_comment'></div>又弱一个，人何望焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1304624_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1304624_comment'></div>官至元士，官不为小；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1304624_comment'></div>年踰耳顺，年不为夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1304624_comment'></div>所可恨者，积丰施眇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1304624_comment'></div>郡失良牧，朝失荩臣，子失名父，里失贤人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1304624_comment'></div>知与不知，怆然伤神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1304624_comment'></div>某也辱知，亶非一日，迎拜素车，有泪盈臆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1304624_comment'></div>卮酒写哀，公其来格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1304624_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_1304624'></div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1304624_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　通判漳州，因应诏言事，削秩免官。作品：《漳州辞庙文》<div id='poem_1304634' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304634' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304634?labeling=true' target='_blank'>漳州辞庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304634")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304634_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304634'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304634'>乙未秋闰，奏对未央。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304634_comment'></div>其未信而谏也似讪，其私忧过计也似狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304634_comment'></div>俯不愧于此心，仰不愧于彼苍，明不负于天子，幽不负于宁皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304634_comment'></div>惟是结怨乎边帅，掇怒乎庙堂，交恶乎阉宦，取谗乎妃嫱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304634_comment'></div>反舟蓬岛，奉祠故乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304634_comment'></div>圣恩宽大，俾倅于漳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304634_comment'></div>敢求言之有诏，将献忠于皂囊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304634_comment'></div>疏已成而未奏，俄白简之飞霜，谓不当谄事真某而慕名胜，交结洪、魏而相誇张；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304634_comment'></div>又不当诋二相之为牛、李，以今日而比有唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304634_comment'></div>以此得罪，分之所当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304634_comment'></div>归处南山之下，读书养正之堂，誓无片言以干时，不作一书以入杭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304634_comment'></div>亦有神明，质之在旁，临行告别，寓诚瓣香，神之听之，绾他肠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1304634_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
井冈山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e1004c558a0e46a38f1c995f7af5784e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e1004c558a0e46a38f1c995f7af5784e");'><span id='e1004c558a0e46a38f1c995f7af5784e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1243')">1241-1243年</a>，58-60岁</div><div id='e1004c558a0e46a38f1c995f7af5784e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1241')">1241年</a>　春，通判吉州，友人刘克庄作诗送之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1242&endYear=1242')">1242年1月</a>　在通判吉州任上。正月，真德秀《政经》作序。作品：《政经序》<div id='poem_1304549' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304549' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304549?labeling=true' target='_blank'>政经序</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳祐二年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304549")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304549_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304549'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304549'>西山先生真文忠公《心经》一书行于世，至彻禁中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304549_comment'></div>端平乙未夏五公薨后两月，从臣洪公舜俞咨夔在经筵，上出公《心经》曰：「真某此书，朕乙夜览而嘉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304549_comment'></div>卿宜为之序」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304549_comment'></div>洪公退，尝与迈言，至相顾陨涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304549_comment'></div>既而洪公亦告瘁，不知是书尝序与否也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304549_comment'></div>今所谓《政经》者，乃先生再守温陵日所著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304549_comment'></div>迈时分教睢邸，乡友赵时棣宗华为法曹，朝夕相与亲炙琴瑟书册之侧，遂得此经，寔在四方门人之先，而四方门人亦未尽见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304549_comment'></div>宗华令大庾，锓梓县斋，以一帙见畀，且俾序于帙端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304549_comment'></div>迈窃谓天下之书多矣，然有之无所补，无之靡所阙者，亦多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304549_comment'></div>先生所著之书，凿凿桑麻谷粟之不可阙者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304549_comment'></div>惟《心经》所以为开天理迪民彝之大本，惟《政经》所以为续天命救民穷之实用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304549_comment'></div>《心经》可以接伊洛之正传，衍朱、张之遗学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304549_comment'></div>《政经》则自体以达用，举而措之事业，小则为程纯公晋城县谱，次则为富文忠公青州郡谱，大则为韩忠献公、司马文正公嘉祐、元祐之相谱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304549_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304549_comment'></div>国步斯频，民亦劳止，有民社者当于《心》、《政》二经佩服而力行之，则民瘼庶其有瘳乎，国脉庶其有永乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304549_comment'></div>淳祐二年月正元日，门人王迈序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1304549_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1243&endYear=1243')">1243年</a>　在通判吉州任上。为仙游县傅氏金石山福神道院作记。作品：《仙游县傅氏金石山福神道院记》<div id='poem_1304585' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1304585' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1304585?labeling=true' target='_blank'>仙游县傅氏金石山福神道院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1243年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_1304585")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1304585_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1304585'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1304585'>金石山福神道院，仙游傅氏所造也，经始于建炎之庚戌，绩成于绍兴之丁巳，中间拓地增屋者不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1304585_comment'></div>淳祐癸卯而后，嗣孙莳嘱甥王迈为文以识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1304585_comment'></div>金石山者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1304585_comment'></div>何以少师公得名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1304585_comment'></div>曷名乎福神道院？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1304585_comment'></div>公之子夔漕作堂祀先而寓名乎福神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1304585_comment'></div>初，少师公未冠，试广文馆为第一，从古灵先生襄游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1304585_comment'></div>时墙屏问道千馀人，先生独曰「傅元通金石人也」，以女妻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1304585_comment'></div>熙宁王、吕锐于变法，道路以目，先生屡为神宗言新法挠民非便，不听则具疏争之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1304585_comment'></div>公所亲告公曰：「时相得君方专，上方举国听之，先生力诋其非，必犯九关虎豹之怒，子于翁婿间宜谏止之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1304585_comment'></div>不然，祸将及子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1304585_comment'></div>公正色曰：「吾师之道正道也，彼相之说邪说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1304585_comment'></div>以正道辟邪说，吾徒当相与张而大之，矧可讽之小贬其道乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1304585_comment'></div>告者语塞，公且为润色谏疏，以明称王、吕之罪，遂为所恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1304585_comment'></div>暨邹道乡以谏官言事得贬，章子厚使人极之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1304585_comment'></div>于其所往，平生故人望望去之，公义形于色曰：「不负杨临贺者何人哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1304585_comment'></div>竟厚赆邹公之行，坐是免所居官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1304585_comment'></div>踰年邹得生还，公亦被召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1304585_comment'></div>曾布牢笼之以助己，公守师说不为之动，布力挤之，于是有亳州之命矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1304585_comment'></div>自是党论日炽，端人庄士之子孙俱罹禁锢之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1304585_comment'></div>公以徽庙旧学仅免窜逐，竟抱杞天之忧，薨于亳，葬于常之宜兴，朝廷赐善权山广教寺以资冥福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1304585_comment'></div>夔漕以公故浮沉州县二十馀年，不敢背教忠之训，以求合于权门也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1304585_comment'></div>尝仕括苍，乘桴而还，遇风涛汹涌，众舟俱覆，顾瞻对岸有北方正神之帜植乎其前，若有物扶之以济于险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1304585_comment'></div>既归仙游，每食必下泪曰：「吾亲松楸在三千里外，虽蒙恩奉香火有所，然为子若孙不能时展烝尝之敬，宁不见诮于马医夏畦之鬼」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1304585_comment'></div>乃捐俸割地，创堂于邑之北山，奉少师祠，以福神名之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1304585_comment'></div>括苍有羽士梅洞霄，于六飞未南渡之前尝言钱塘有天子气，既而言验，携与偕来，是为开山之祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1304585_comment'></div>铸钟累月不就，陈夫人投金钗于炉而钟成，叩之无声，梅挥剑击之，声始大震，至今一钗一剑之痕隐隐浮于蹲熊盘龙之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1304585_comment'></div>故斯堂虽为祠先，而亦为四方水旱禳禬之地，此记之不容已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1304585_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1304585_comment'></div>生天地间，非亲何爱，非君何尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1304585_comment'></div>师也者教之孝以事其亲，忠以事其君，昭昭乎在三之义，人极之所以立、人类之所以蕃者，其不在兹乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1304585_comment'></div>惟少师公事师尽道，事君尽言，不以时之燥湿而为趋背，不以身之升沉而为戚欣，盖不忍于叛师而忘君也，故未尝染刘舆之腻而污元规之尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1304585_comment'></div>惟夔漕公事生以礼，事亡如存，一饮食不忘南陔之兰，一跬步必顾太行之云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1304585_comment'></div>故揭名妥灵于斯堂也，恍乎音容之若见，忾乎謦咳之有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1304585_comment'></div>夫是之谓忠臣孝子，萃于傅氏之门，虽附益之以道家之说，若祭之邻于非鬼，语之涉于怪神，然因亲以寓名，君子亦可观过以知仁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1304585_comment'></div>夫忠孝之后必大，二公往矣，出乎其系者露颖于童科，充赋于国宾，策勋兰省而对策于天子之庭者，代不乏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1304585_comment'></div>继自今丰末以培其本，疏流以浚其源，使锡类之孝、体国之忠，明可以刑善于乡国，幽可以对越于乾坤，是又二公洋洋之灵所期望于百世之子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1304585_comment'></div>迈傅之所自出，故大书特书之，使来者有考于斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1304585_comment'></div>少师公讳某，字元通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1304585_comment'></div>夔漕公讳谦受，字冲亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1304585_comment'></div>道院之址载于傅氏之质剂，岁自输租于官，住堂听自择，有司不与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1304585_comment'></div>东偏旧有岳殿，今撤而新之，乃傅知琳所董云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1304585_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1243&endYear=1243')">1243年</a>　有词与友人王伯大唱和。作品：《摸鱼儿》（昔元城、一生清峭）<div id='poem_71377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>摸鱼儿 闽漕王幼学作碧湾丹嶂堂，歌此词，以墨本见寄，依韵和之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1243年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30426, "南宋", "王迈", "poem_title_71377")'>王迈</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_71377_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_71377'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71377'>昔元城、一生清峭，南都高卧坚壁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71377'>留耕便是元城样，何肯枉吾寻尺。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71377'>曾直笔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71377'>说社稷安危，屡叩龙墀额。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71377'>明时逐客。<div id='poem_sentence_4_71377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_71377'>却惠顾丹山，来持翠节，对此一湾碧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_71377_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_71377'>澄清暇，无奈登临有癖。<div id='poem_sentence_6_71377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_71377'>梅山时访仙迹。<div id='poem_sentence_7_71377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_71377'>神仙偏喜公心事，一见莞然前席。<div id='poem_sentence_8_71377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_71377'>闲不得。<div id='poem_sentence_9_71377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_71377'>有先见蓍龟，消得君王忆。<div id='poem_sentence_10_71377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_71377'>天阍不隔。<div id='poem_sentence_11_71377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_71377'>要济险孤舟，支倾一柱，公外向谁觅。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_71377_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
邵武
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='97c27455de904dd2a7b87f131b85fa68_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("97c27455de904dd2a7b87f131b85fa68");'><span id='97c27455de904dd2a7b87f131b85fa68_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1247')">1244-1247年</a>，61-64岁</div><div id='97c27455de904dd2a7b87f131b85fa68' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年</a>　知邵武军。有词为刘克庄母夫人84岁祝寿。作品：《贺新郎•为后村母夫人寿》<div id='poem_71372' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71372' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71372?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新郎<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>为后村母夫人寿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1244年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71372'>看花冠、端容丽服，补陀岩主。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71372'>只坐尘缘蹉一念，朱紫丛中得度。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71372'>人世福、夫人兼五。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71372'>银鹿诸孙来定省，对金屏、绣幕辉云母。<div id='poem_sentence_4_71372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_71372'>人顶礼，柳行路<span id='poem_sentence_9_71372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_71372'>上殿肩舆帘蹙绣，遣佳儿、扶掖天应许。<div id='poem_sentence_10_71372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_71372'>笑陈媪，三题柱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_71372_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1245&endYear=1245')">1245年</a>　知邵武军，作劝粜歌，民赖以济，民甚德之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年</a>　知邵武军。右言正江万里荐其才可用，未果。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年</a>　与同僚宴于熙春台，有词纪之。作品：《念奴娇•熙春台宴同官》<div id='poem_71370' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71370' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_71370'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71370'>层台云外，阅古今、多少兴衰成败。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71370'>老木千章，若个是、南国甘棠遗爱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71370'>群籁号风，繁阴蔽日，有此清凉界。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71370'>宾朋在坐，朗然心目明快。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71370_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71370'>更向会景亭前，登高吊古，此景何人会。<div id='poem_sentence_4_71370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_71370'>岁岁春来春又去，独有灵台春在。<div id='poem_sentence_5_71370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_71370'>早稻炊香，晚禾摇穗，管取三登泰。<div id='poem_sentence_6_71370_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_71370'>酿成春酒，把杯行乐须再。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_71370_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年</a>　在邵武任上。与同僚宴，有词纪之。作品：《贺新郎•丁未守邵武宴同官》<div id='poem_71373' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71373' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71373'>觉朝来、薰风满入，生绡团扇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71373_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71373'>太守愁眉才一展，且喜街头米贱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_71373_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_71373'>家山乐事真堪羡。<div id='poem_sentence_6_71373_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_71373_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_71373'>笑富贵、都如邮传。<div id='poem_sentence_9_71373_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_71373_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年5月</a>　是年五月，方大琮（字德潤）卒，为撰行状。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年</a>　知邵武军。以左曹郎官召，力辞，除直秘阁广东提举，再辞。改侍右郎官，未行予祠。<br /></div>
